+++
title = "३"
+++

(3.1)



## **manvantara-vivaraṇam**

**śrī-maitreya uvāca—**  
**kathitā guruṇā samyag-bhū-samudrādi-saṁsthitiḥ |**  
**sūryādīnāṁ ca saṁsthānaṁ jyotiṣāṁ cātivistarāt ||1||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: 

parānandapadāmbhoja-śrīdharaḥ śrīdharo yatiḥ |   
purāṇe vaiṣṇave vyākhyāt tṛtīyāṁśe yathāmati ||   
aṁśadvayena sṛṣṭyādidvisaptabhuvanoktibhiḥ |   
adhyāropya niṣiddhaṁ tad rājadvijasaduktibhiḥ ||   
tṛtīyāṁśe manuvyāsadharmādyāḥ sthitihetavaḥ |   
varṇyante'tra niṣedhāya kauravyapṛtanā yathā ||   
atrāpi prathame'dhyāye saptamanvantarāṇi tu |   
bhavadbhūtāni kathitānyavatārā harerapi || 

vṛttakīrtanapūrvakaṁ manvantarāṇāṁ svarūpaṁ pṛcchati—kathitā iti caturbhiḥ ||1|| 

**devādīnāṁ tathā sṛṣṭir ṛṣīṇāṁcāpi varṇitā |**  
**cāturvarṇyasya cotpattis tiryag-yoni-gatasya ca ||2||**

**dhruva-prahrāda-caritaṁ vistārāc ca tvayoditam |**  
**manvantarāṇy aśeṣāṇi śrotum icchāmyanukramāt ||3||**

**manvantarādhipāṁś caiva śakra-deva-purogamān |**  
**bhavatā kathitān etān śrotum icchāmy ahaṁ guro ||4||**

**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**  
**atītān āgatānīha yāni manvantarāṇi vai |**  
**tāny ahaṁ bhavataḥ samyak kathayāmi yathā-kramam ||5||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: iha vārāhakalpe | yathākramamityanena kramaprāptaṁ vartamānamapi manvantaraṁ jñeyam ||5||

**svāyambhuvo manuḥ pūrvaṁ paraḥ svārociṣas tathā |**  
**uttamas tāmasaś caiva raivataś cākṣuṣas tathā ||6||**

**ṣaḍ ete manavo’tītāḥ sāmprataṁ tu raveḥ sutaḥ |**  
**vaivasvato’yaṁ yasyaitat saptamaṁ vartate’ntaram ||7||**

**svāyambhuvaṁ tu kathitaṁ kalpādāv antaraṁ mayā |**  
**devāḥ saptarṣayaś caiva yathāvat kathitā mayā ||8||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: kalpasya ādau svāyambhuvamanvantarantu kathitaṁ, prathamāṁśe devā yāmākhyā ṛṣayo marīcyādayaḥ | cakārādindro yajñaḥ | manuputrau priyavratottānapādau kathitau ||8||

**ata ūrdhvaṁ pravakṣyāmi manoḥ svārociṣasya tu |**  
**manvantarādhipān samyag devarṣīṁs tat-sutāṁs tathā ||9||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: devarṣīn devān ṛṣīṁśca tatsutān manuputrān ||9|| 

**pārāvatāḥ satuṣitā devāḥ svārociṣe’ntare |**  
**vipaścit tatra devendro maitreyāsīn mahābalaḥ ||10||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: pārāvatāstuṣitāśca devagaṇau vipaścit saṁjño devendraḥ ||10|| 

**ūrjaḥ stambhas tathā prāṇo vāto’tha pṛṣabhas tathā |**  
**nirayaś ca parīvāṁś ca tatra saptarṣayo’bhavan ||11||**

**caitra-kimpuruṣādyāś ca sutāḥ svārociṣasya tu |**  
**dvitīyam etad-vyākhyātam antaraṁ śṛṇu cottamam ||12||**

**tṛtīye’py antare brahmann uttamo nāma yo manuḥ |**  
**suśāntir nāma devendro maitreyāsīt sureśvaraḥ ||13||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: uttamam uttamasambandhi manvantaram | uttama evauttamiḥ ||12-13|| 

**sudhāmānas tathā satyā japāśvātha pratardanāḥ |**  
**vaśavartinaś ca pañcaite gaṇādvādaśakāḥ smṛtāḥ ||14||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: dvādaśakāḥ dvādaśānāṁ ekaiko gaṇaḥ ityevamete pañca gaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ ||14|| 

**vasiṣṭha-tanayā hy ete sapta saptarṣayo’bhavan |**  
**ajaḥ paraśu-dīptādyās tathottama-manoḥ sutāḥ ||15||**

**tāmasasyāntare devāḥ supārā harayas tathā |**  
**satyāś ca sudhiyaś caiva saptaviṁśatikā gaṇāḥ ||16||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: saptaviṁśatikāḥ saptaviṁśatīnāṁ gaṇāḥ ||16||

**śivirindras tathā cāsīc chatayajñopalakṣaṇaḥ |**  
**saptarṣayaś ca ye teṣāṁ teṣāṁ nāmāni me śṛṇu ||17||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: śatayajñopalakṣaṇaḥ śatakratuḥ | atra tāmase manvantare ye saptarṣayaḥ teṣāṁ nāmāni me śṛṇu ityanvayaḥ ||17||

**jyotir dhāmā pṛthuḥ kāvyaś caitro’gnir vanakas tathā |**  
**pīvaraś ca rṣayo hy ete sapta tatrāpi cāntare ||18||**

**naraḥ khyātiḥ ketu-rūpo jānu-jaṅghādayas tathā |**  
**putrās tu tāmasasyāsan rpajānaḥ sumahābalāḥ ||19||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: jyotirdhāmetyanvarthakaṁ nāma ||19|| 

**pañcame vāpi maitreya raivato nāma nāmataḥ |**  
**manur vibhuś ca tatrendro devāṁś cātrāntare śṛṇu ||20||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: raivato nāma nāmata iti—nāma-prasiddhau, nāmataḥ saṁjñayaiva, na tu revataputraḥ ||20|| 

**amitābhā bhūtarayā vaikuṇṭhāḥ sama-medhasaḥ |**  
**ete deva-gaṇās tatra caturdaśa caturdaśa ||21||**

**hiraṇyaromāveda-śrīr ūrdhva-bāhus tathāparaḥ |**  
**veda-bāhuḥ sudhāmā ca parjanyaś ca mahāmuniḥ |**  
**ete saptarṣayo vipra tatrāsan raivate’ntare ||22||**

**bala-bandhuś ca sambhāvyaḥ satyakādyāś ca tat-sutāḥ |**  
**narendrāś ca mahāvīryā babhūvur muni-sattama ||23||**

**svārociṣaś cottamaś ca tāmaso raivatas tathā |**  
**priyavratānvayā hy ete catvāro manavaḥ smṛtāḥ ||24||**

**viśeṣphalsarvum ārādhya tapasā sa rājarṣiḥ priyavrataḥ |**  
**manvantarādhipān etān labdhavān ātma-vaṁśajān ||25||**

**ṣaṣṭhe manvantare cāsīc cākṣuṣākhyas tathā manuḥ |**  
**manojavas tathaivendro devān api nibodha me ||26||**

**amitābhā bhūtarajovaikuṇṭhāḥ sasumedhasaḥ |**  
**ete devagaṇāstatra caturdaśa caturdaśa ||21||**

**hiraṇyaromā devaśrīrūrddhvabāhustathāparaḥ |**  
**vedabāhuḥ sudhāmā ca parjanyaśca mahāmuniḥ |**  
**ete saptarṣayo vipra tatrāsan raivate'ntare ||22||**

**balabandhuḥ susambhāruḥ satyakādyāśca tatsutāḥ |**  
**narendrāḥ sumahāvīryā babhūvurmunisattama ||23||**

**svārociṣaścauttamiśca tāmaso raivatastathā |**  
**priyavratānvayā hyete catvāro manavastathā ||24||**

**viṣṇumārādhya tapasā sa rājarṣiḥ priyavrataḥ |**  
**manvantarādhipānetān labdhavānātmavaṁśajān ||25||**

**ṣaṣṭhe manvantare cāsīccākṣuṣākhyastathā manuḥ |**  
**manojavastathaivendro devānapi nibodha me ||26||**

**ādyāḥ prasūtā bhavyāśca pṛthugāśca divaukasaḥ |**  
**mahānubhāvā lekhāśca pañcaite'pyaṣṭakā ganāḥ ||27||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: pratyekaṁ caturdaśabhūtā ete gaṇāḥ ||22-27||

**sumedhā virajāścaiva haviṣmānuttamo madhuḥ |**  
**atināmā sahiṣṇuśca saptāsanniti carṣayaḥ ||28||**

**ūruḥ puruḥ śatadyumnapramukhāḥ sumahābalāḥ |**  
**cākṣuṣasya manoḥ putrāḥ pṛthivīpatayo'bhavan ||29||**

**vivasvataḥ suto vipra śrāddhadevo mahādyutiḥ |**  
**manuḥ saṁvarttate dhīmān sāmprataṁ saptame'ntare ||30||**

**āditya-vasu-rudrādyā devāścātra mahāmune**  
**purandarastathaivātra maitreya tridaśeśvaraḥ ||31||**

**vasiṣṭhaḥ kāśyapo'thātrirjamadagniḥ sagautamaḥ |**  
**viśvāmitro bharadvājaḥ sapta saptarṣayo'bhavan ||32||**

**ikṣvākuścaiva nābhāgo dhṛṣṭaḥ śayatireva ca |**  
**nariṣyantaśca vikhyāto nābha uddiṣṭa eva ca ||33||**

**karūśaśca pṛṣadhraśca vasumān lokaviśrutaḥ |**  
**manorvaivasvatasyaite nava putrāśca dhārmikāḥ ||34||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vasumān lokaviśruta iti viśeṣaṇadvayam | pṛṣadhraścaiva vasumān vīryavān vasiṣṭhaśāpe jñāte'pi kṣobhābhāvāt | lokaviśrutaḥ sarvasaṅgaparityāgena muktiprāpteḥ | tathā sati nava putrā mahābalā iti navatvam upapannaṁ bhavati ||34|| 

**viṣṇuśaktiranaupamyā sattvodriktā sthitau sthitā |**  
**manvantareṣvaśeṣeṣu devatvenādhitiṣṭhati ||35||**

**aṁśena tasya jajñe'sau yajñaḥ svāyambhuve'ntare |**  
**ākṛtyāṁ mānaso deva utpannaḥ prathame'ntare ||36||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: evaṁ tarhi manuputradevendrarṣibhiḥ pañcabhireva jagataḥ pālane siddhe kṛtaṁ viṣṇoḥ pālakatvena ityāśaṅkya sarveṣvapi manvantareṣu pālane pravṛttasya viṣṇoradhiṣṭhātṛtvaṁ darśayati—viṣṇuśaktir ityādinā yāvadadhyāyasamāptiḥ | devayajñādirūpadevatābhāvena viṣṇoḥ svarūpabhūtā śaktiḥ, tasya viṣṇoḥ aṁśena svāyambhuvamanvantare ākūtyāṁ mātari yajñasaṁjñaḥ utpannaḥ jajñe babhūvetyarthaḥ yadvā prathame antare avasare brahmaṇo mānasaḥ yaḥ utpanno ruciḥ tasmāt pituḥ jajñe iti ||35-36||

**tataḥ punaḥ sa vai devaḥ prāpte svārociṣe'ntare |**  
**tuṣitāyāṁ samutpanno hyajitastuṣitaiḥ saha ||37||**

**auttame tvantare caiva tuṣitastu punaḥ sa vai |**  
**satyāyāmabhavat satyaḥ satyaiḥ saha surottamaiḥ ||38||**

**tāmasasyāntare caiva samprāpte punareva hi |**  
**haryāyāṁ haribhiḥ sārdha harireva babhūva ha ||39||**

**raivate'pyantare devaḥ sambhūtyāṁ mānaso'bhavat |**  
**sambhūto raivataiḥ sārdhaṁ devairdevavaro hariḥ ||40||**

**cākṣuṣe cāntare devo vaikuṇṭhaḥ puruṣottamaḥ |**  
**vikuṇṭhāyāmasau jajñe vaikuṇṭhairdaivataiḥ saha ||41||**

**manvantare tu samprāpte tathā vaivasvate dvija |**  
**vāmanaḥ kaśyapād viṣṇuradityāṁ sambabhūva ha ||42||**

**tribhiḥ kramairimāllokāñjitvā yena mahātmanā |**  
**purandarāya trailokyaṁ dattaṁ nihatakaṇṭakam||43||**

**ityetāstanavastasya saptamanvantareṣu vai |**  
**saptāthavābhavan vipra yābhiḥ saṁvarddhitāḥ prajāḥ ||44||**

**yasmād viśvamidaṁ sarvaṁ tasya śaktyā mahātmanaḥ |**  
**tasmād sa procyate viṣṇurviśerdhātoḥ praveśanāt ||45||**

**sarve ca devā manavaḥ samastāḥ saptarṣayo ye manusūnavaśca |**  
**indraśca yo'yaṁ tridaśeśabhūto viṣṇoraśeṣāstu vibhūtayastāḥ ||46||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: uktameva arthaṁ viṣṇupadaniruktyā darśayan manvādiṣu ca tadāveśam āha—yasmād iti dvābhyām | mahātmanaḥ śaktyā svarūpabhūtayā praveśanāt praveśanārthāt ||46|| 

iti śrīdhara-kṛtāyām ātma-prakāśākhyāyāṁ svaprakāśākhyāyāṁ vā śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇa-ṭīkāyāṁ tṛtīyāṁśe prathamo'dhyāyaḥ ||

|| iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe tṛtīye’ṁśe prathamo’dhyāyaḥ ||

—o)0(o—

(3.2)



## **sāvarṇyādi-manvantara-kathanaṁ, kalpa-parimāṇaṁ ca**

**śrī-maitreya uvāca—**  
**proktāny etāni bhavatā sapta-manvantarāṇi vai |**  
**bhaviṣyāṇy api viprarṣe mamākhyātuṁ tvam arhasi ||1||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: dvitīye sapta manvādīn vakṣyannādau raveḥ sutaḥ | yathā sāvarṇirabhavaditihāsaṁ tamabravīt ||1|| 

**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**  
**sūryasya patnī saṁjñābhuttamt tanayā viśvakarmaṇaḥ |**  
**manur yamo yamī caiva tad-apatyāni vai mune ||2||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: manuḥ śrāddhadevaḥ ||2|| 

**asahantī tu sā bhartus tejaś chāyāṁ yuyoja vai |**  
**bhartṛ-śuśrūṣaṇe’raṇyaṁ svayaṁ ca tapase yayau ||3||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: chāyāṁ bimbatulyāṁ svasadṛśīmanyāṁ striyaṁ sūryatejaḥsahiṣṇuṁ nirmāya bhartuḥ śuśrūṣaṇe yuyoja, svayañca tapase yayāvityarthaḥ ||3||

**saṁjñeyam ity athārkaś ca chāyāyām ātmaja-trayam |**  
**śanaiścaraṁ manuṁ cānyaṁ tapatīṁ cāpy ajījanat ||4||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: atra manuṁ sāvarṇim | tapatīṁ saṁvaraṇasya rājño bhāryām ||4|| 

**chāyā-saṁjñā dadau śāpaṁ yamāya kupitā yadā |**  
**tadānyeyam asau buddhir ty āsīd yama-sūryayoḥ ||5||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: chāyaiva saṁjñārūpeṇa sthitā chāyāsaṁjñā | sā kadācit svāpatyatrayasnehavatī ātmani pādaprahārodyatāya yamāya pādaste patatviti śāpaṁ dadau | tadātinirdayatvamālakṣya neyamasau saṁjñā, kintu anyeyaṁ saṁhoti yamasūryayorbaddhirabhūdityarthaḥ ||5||

**tato vivasvān ākhyāte tayaivāraṇya-saṁsthitām |**  
**samādhi-dṛṣṭyā dadṛśe tām aśvāṁ tapasi sthitām ||6||**

**vāji-rūpa-dharaḥ so’yaṁ tasyāṁ devāv athāśvinau |**  
**janayāmāsa revantaṁ retaso’nte ca bhāskaraḥ ||7||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tataścātinirbandhaṁ pṛṣṭayā tayā nāhaṁ saṁjñā kintu tasyāśchāyeti ākhyāte vivasvān sūryaḥ samādhinottarakuruṣvaraṇye aśvāṁ vaḍavārūpāṁ tapasi sthitāṁ saṁjñāṁ dadṛśe dadarśa | tataḥ so'pi vivasvānaśvarūpadharastasyāmaśvinau devau revantañceti trayamajījanat | retaso'nta iti revantanāmaniruktiḥ ||7||

**āninye ca punaḥ saṁjñāṁ sva-sthānaṁ bhagavān raviḥ |**  
**tejasaḥ śamanaṁ cāsya viśvakarmā cakāra ha ||8||**

**bhramam āropya sūryaṁ tu tasya tejo-niśātanam |**   
**kṛtavān aṣṭamaṁ bhāgaṁ sa vyaśrīātayad avyayam ||9||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: bhramiṁ cakrākāraṁ takṣayantram | tejaso viśātanaṁ kṛtavān | aṣṭamaṁ bhāgaṁ na vyaśātayat yato'vyayam ||9||

**yat tasmād vaiṣānāṁavaṁ tejaḥ-śātitaṁ viśvakarmaṇā |**  
**jājvalyamānam apatat tad-bhūmau muni-sattama ||10||**

**tvasarvsthitaiva tejasā tena visarvānāṁośrī cakram akalpayat |**  
**triśūlaṁ caiva śarvasya śivikāṁ dhanadasya ca ||11||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: dhanadasya śibikāyantram ||11|| 

**śaktiṁ guhasya devānām anyeṣāṁ ca yad-āyudham |**  
**tat sarvaṁ tejasā tena viśvakarmā vyavardhayat ||12||**

**chāyā-saṁjñā-suto yo’sau dvitīyaḥ kathito manuḥ |**  
**pūrvajasya sarvarṇo’sau sāvarṇis tena kathyate ||13||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: pūrvajasya śrāddhadevasya savarṇaḥ manuriti samānavarṇatvāt sūryaputratvāt tulyarūpatvāddhā ||13|| 

**tasya manvantaraṁ he etat sāvarṇikam athāṣṭamam |**  
**tac chṛṇuṣva mahābhāga bhaviṣyat kathayāmi te ||14||**

**sāvarṇis tu manur yo’sau maitreya bhavitā tataḥ |**  
**sutapāś cāmitābhāś ca mukhyāśrī cāpi tathā surāḥ ||15||**

**teṣāṁ gaṇaś ca devānāṁ ekaiko viṁśakaḥ smṛtaḥ |**  
**saptarṣīn api vakṣyāmi bhaviṣyān muni-sattama ||16||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: viṁśakaḥ viṁśatisaṁkhyakaḥ ||16||

**dīptimān gālavo rāmaḥ kṛpo drauṇis tathā paraḥ |**  
**mat-putraś ca tathā vyāsa ṛṣyaśṛṅgaś ca saptamaḥ ||17||**

**viṣṇu-prasādād anaghaḥ pātālāntara-gocaraḥ |**  
**virocana-sutas teṣāṁ balir indro bhaviṣyati ||18||**

**virajāś corvarīvāṁś ca nirmokādyās tathāpare |**  
**sāvarṇes tu manoḥ putrā bhaviṣyanti nareśvarāḥ ||19||**

**navamo dakṣa-sāvarṇir bhaviṣyati mune manuḥ ||20||**

**pārā marīci-garbhāś ca sudharmāṇas tathā tridhā |**  
**bhaviṣyanti tathā devā hy ekaiko dvādaśo gaṇaḥ ||21||**

**teṣāṁ indro mahā-vīryo bhaviṣyaty adbhuto dvija ||22||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: adbhutasaṁjñaḥ indraḥ ||22|| 

**savano dyutimān bhavyo vasur medhātithis tathā |**  
**jyotiṣmān saptamaḥ satyas tatraite ca maharṣayaḥ ||23||**

**dhṛtaketur dīptiketuḥ pañca-hasta-nirāmayau |**  
**pṛthuśravādyāś ca tathā dakṣa-sāvarṇikātmajāḥ ||24||**

**daśamo brahma-sāvarṇir bhaviṣyati mune manuḥ |**  
**sudhāmāno viśuddhāś ca śata-saṅkhyās tathā surāḥ ||25||**

**teṣāṁ indraś ca bhavitā śāntir nāma mahā-balaḥ |**  
**saptarṣayo bhaviṣyanti ye tathā tān śṛṇuṣva ha ||26||**

**haviṣmān sukṛtaḥ satyas tapo-mūrtis tathāparaḥ |**  
**nābhogo’pratimaujāś ca satyaketus tathaiva ca ||27||**

**sukṣetraś cottamaujāś ca bhūriṣeṇādayo daśa |**  
**brahma-sāvarṇi-putrās tu rakṣiṣyanti vasundharām ||28||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: sukṣetrādayaḥ brahmāsāvarṇiputrāḥ ||28||

**ekādaśaś ca bhavitā dharma-sāvarṇiko manuḥ ||29||**

**vihaṅgamāḥ kāmagamā nirvāṇa-ratayas tathā |**  
**gaṇās tv ete tadā mukhyā devānāṁ ca bhaviṣyatām |**  
**ekaikas triṁśakas teṣāṁ gaṇaś cendraś ca vai vṛṣaḥ ||30||**

**niḥsvaraś cāgni-tejāś ca vapuṣmān ghṛṇir āruṇiḥ |**  
**haviṣmān anaghaś caiva bhāvyāḥ saptarṣayas tathā ||31||**

**sarvatra-gaḥ sudharmā ca devānīkādayas tathā |**  
**bhaviṣyanti manos tasya tanayāḥ pṛthivīśvarāḥ ||32||**

**rudra-putras tu sāvarṇir bhavitā dvādaśo manuḥ |**  
**ṛtudhāmā ca tatrendro bhavitā śṛṇu me surān ||33||**

**haritā rohitā devās tathā samunaso dvija |**  
**sukarmāṇaḥ surāpāś ca daśakāḥ pañca vai gaṇāḥ ||34||**

**tapasvī sutapaś caiva tapo-mūrtis tapo-ratiḥ |**  
**tapo-dhṛtir dyutiś cānyaḥ saptamas tu tapo-dhanaḥ |**  
**saptarṣayas tv ime tasya putrān api nibodha me ||35||**

**devavān upadevaś ca deva-śreṣṭhādayas tathā |**  
**manos tasya mahāvīryā bhaviṣyanti mahānṛpāḥ ||36||**

**trayodaśo rucir nāmā bhaviṣyati mune manuḥ ||37||**

**sutrāmāṇaḥ sukarmāṇaḥ sudharmāṇas taṣṭamarāḥ |**  
**trayastriṁśad-vibhedās te devānāṁ yatra vai gaṇāḥ ||38||**

**dviaspatir mahā-vīryas teṣāṁ indro bhaviṣyati ||39||**

**nirmohas tattva-darśīca niṣprakampyo nirutsukaḥ |**  
**dhṛtimān avyayaś cānyaḥ saptamaḥ sutapā muniḥ |**  
**saptarṣayas tv amī tasya putrān api nibodha me ||40||**

**citrasena-vicitrādyā bhaviṣyanti mahīkṣitaḥ ||41||**

**bhaumaś caturdaśaś cātra maitreya bhaviṣyati1 manuḥ |**  
**śucir indraḥ sura-gaṇās tatra pañca śṛṇuṣva tān ||42||**

**cākṣuṣāś ca pavitrāś ca kaniṣṭhā bhrājikās tathā |**  
**vācā vṛddhāś ca vai devāḥ saptarṣīn api me śṛṇu ||43||**

**agnibāhuḥ śuciḥ śukro māgadho’gnidhra eva ca |**  
**yuktas tathā jitaś cānyo manu-putrān ataḥ śṛṇu ||44||**

**ūrugambhīra-buddhyādyā manos tasya sutā nṛpāḥ |**  
**kathitā muni-śārdūla pālayiṣyanti ye mahīm ||45||**

**caturyugānte vedānāṁ jāyate kila viplavaḥ |**  
**pravartayanti tān etya bhuvaṁ saptarṣayo divaḥ ||46||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: uktānāṁ manvādīnāṁ kṛtyabhedānāha—caturyugānta iti | kalau vedānāṁ viplave ucchede jāte diviṣṭhā maharṣayo bhuvametya kṛtayugādau tāneva sampravarttayanti ||46||

**kṛte kṛte smṛter vipra praṇetā jāyate manuḥ |**  
**devā yajñabhujas te tu yāvan manvantaraṁ tu tat ||47||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vedapravarttanamuktvā smṛtipravarttanam āha—kṛta iti | smṛteḥ dharmaśāstrasya manusaṁjñasya, tattadṛṣipravartitānāṁ smṛtīnāmupalakṣaṇametat | tattanmanvantare ye devāḥ kīrttitāste tannāmānaḥ tattanmanvantare yajñabhujo bhavanti | yāvanmanvantaraṁ manvantarasamāptiparyantam ||47||

**bhavanti ye manoḥ putrā yāvan manvantaraṁ tu taiḥ |**  
**tad-anvayodbhavaiś caiva tāvad bhūḥ paripālyate ||48||**

**manuḥ saptarṣayo devā bhūpālāś ca manoḥ sutāḥ |**  
**manvantare bhavanty ete śakraś caivādhikāriṇaḥ ||49||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: anye'pi manvādayastanmanvantarādhikāriṇa eva ityāha manur iti ||49|| 

**caturdaśabhir etais tu gatair manvantarair dvija |**  
**sahasra-yuga-paryantaḥ kalpo niḥśeṣa ucyate ||50||**

**tāvat-pramāṇā ca niśā tato bhavati sattama |**  
**brahma-rūpa-dharaḥ śete śeṣāhāv ambu-samplave ||51||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tāvatpramāṇā ca niśeti—tadā sūryādiparispandarūpa kālopādhyabhāve'pi bhagavato yoganidrārūpamāyopādhiparicchinnasya kālasya tāvattvaṁ jñeyam | brahmeti—divā brahmarūpadharo yaḥ sa eva bhagavān rātrau śrīnārāṇarūpeṇa śeṣāhau anantanāmni sarpa śete ityarthaḥ ||51||

**trailokyam akhilaṁ grastvā bhagavān ādikṛd vibhuḥ |**  
**sva-māyā-sthito vipra sarva-bhūto janārdanaḥ ||52||**

**tataḥ prabuddho bhagavān yathā pūrvaṁ tathā punaḥ |**  
**sṛṣṭiṁ karoty avyayātmā kalpe kalpe rajo-guṇaḥ ||53||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: evameva sarvakalpamanvantarādisthitiṁ saprapañcam āha—tataḥ prabuddhe ityādinā yāvadadhyāyasamāptiḥ ||53|| 

**manavo bhūbhujaḥ sendrā devāḥ saptarṣayas tathā |**  
**sāttviko’ṁśaḥ sthitikaro jagato dvija-sattama ||54||**

**catur-yuge’py asau viṣṇuḥ sthiti-vyāpāra-lakṣaṇaḥ |**  
**yuga-vyavasthāṁ kurute yathā maitreya tac chṛṇu ||55||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: sthitaye yo vyāpāraḥ sa eva lakṣaṇaṁ upādhiryasya saḥ ||55|| 

**kṛte yuge param jñānaṁ kapilādi-svarūpa-dhṛk |**  
**dadāti sarva-bhūtātmā sarva-bhūta-hite rataḥ ||56||**

**cakravarti-svarūpeṇa tretāyāṁ api sa prabhuḥ |**  
**duṣṭānāṁ nigrahaṁ kurvan paripāti jagat-trayam ||57||**

**vedam ekaṁ catur-bhedaṁ kṛtvā śākhā-śatair vibhuḥ |**  
**karoti bahulaṁ bhūyo veda-vyāsa-svarūpa-dhṛk ||58||**

**vedāṁs tu dvāpare vyasya kaler ante punar hariḥ |**  
**kalki-svarūpī durvṛttān mārge khyāpayati prabhuḥ ||59||**

**evam etaj jagat sarvaṁ śaśvat pāti karoti ca |**  
**hanti cānteṣv anantātmā nāsty asmād vyatireki yat ||60||**

**bhūtaṁ bhavyaṁ bhaviṣyaṁ ca sarva-bhūtān mahātmanaḥ |**  
**tad atrānyatra vā vipra sad-bhāvaḥ kathitas tava ||61||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: upasaṁharati—evam iti dvābhyām | atra vā anyatra vā kalpādau tasmāt vyatireki yat bhūtādi, tannāsti, kintu bhedakalpanāśūnyo bhagavānevāstītyeṣa eva sadbhāvaḥ paramārthaḥ kathita iti ||58-59|| 

iti śrīdhara-kṛtāyām ātma-prakāśākhyāyāṁ svaprakāśākhyāyāṁ vā śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇa-ṭīkāyāṁ tṛtīyāṁśe dvitīyo'dhyāyaḥ ||

**manvantarāṇy aśeṣāṇi kathitāni mayā tava |**  
**manvantarādhipāṁś caiva kim anyat kathayāmi te ||62||**

|| iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe tṛtīye’ṁśe dvitīyo’dhyāyaḥ ||

—o)0(o—

(3.3)



## **veda-vyāsasyāṣṭāviṁśati-nāma-kathanam**

**maitreya uvāca—**  
**jñātam etan mayā tvatto yathā sarvam idaṁ jagat |**  
**viṣṇur viṣṇau viṣṇutaś ca na param vidyate tataḥ ||1||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: sthitihetuprasaṅgena muneḥ praśnānusārataḥ | vedavyāsastṛtīye'tra saprapañco'nuvarṇyate | vedavyastiṁ praṣṭuṁ sarvagranthatātparyamanuvadati—jñātam iti | yathā sarvaṁ jagat viṣṇureva, tataḥ paraṁ na vidyate, yathā ca viṣṇo tiṣṭhati, viṣṇauḥ sakāśāt yathā bhavati, tathā tvatto mayā jñātam | anena sarvo'pi kārakādyartho viṣṇāvupalakṣyate ||1|| 

**etat tu śrotum icchāmi vyastā vedā mahātmanā |**  
**vedavyāsa-svarūpeṇa tathā tena yuge yuge ||2||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: yathā vedā vyastā iti prakārapraśnaḥ ||2|| 

**yasmin yasmin yuge vyāso yo ya āsīn mahāmune |**  
**taṁ tam ācakṣva bhagavan śākhābhedāṁś ca me vada ||3||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: yasmin yasminnityadhikaraṇapraśnaḥ | yo ya iti kartṛ praśnaḥ | śākhābhedāniti śākhāsaṁkhyānāmnoḥ praśnaḥ ||3||

**parāśara uvāca—**  
**veda-drumasya maitreya śākhā-bhedāḥ sahasraśaḥ |**  
**na śakto vistarād vaktuṁ saṅkṣepeṇa śṛṇuṣva tam ||4||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tatra tāvat śākhābhedānāṁ saṁkhyāto nāmataśca vistāro vaktumaśakya ityāha—vedadrumasya iti ||4||

**dvāpare dvāpare viṣṇur vyāsa-rūpī mahā-mune |**  
**vedam ekaṁ subahudhā kurute jagato hitaḥ ||5||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: adhikaraṇakartṛsvarūpapraśnayoruttaram āha—dvāpara iti dvābhyām ||5|| 

**vīryaṁ tejo balaṁ cālpaṁ manuṣāṇāṁ avekṣya ca |**  
**hitāya sarva-bhūtānāṁ veda-bhedān karoti saḥ ||6||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vīryamutsāhaḥ, tejaḥ prāgalbhyaṁ, balañcaṁ grahaṇasāmarthyamalpamavekṣya ||6|| 

**yayāsau kurute tanvā vedam ekaṁ pṛthak prabhuḥ |**  
**vedavyāsābhidhānā tu sā ca mūrtir madhudviṣaḥ ||7||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: nanu apara eva vedavyāsāḥ, kathaṁ bhagavān vedabhedān karoti ityāśaṁkya—sarve bhagavattanava ityāha—yaya iti ||7||

**yasmin manvantare vyāsā ye ye syus tān nibodha me |**  
**yathā ca bhedaḥ śākhānāṁ vyāsena kriyate mune ||8||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: atra tāvat atītānāgatamanvantarāṇāṁ vyāsān ativistaratvena upekṣya vaivasvate manvantare vyatītān vyāsān bhāvinañcaikaṁ tathā śākhābhedāṁśca vaktum āha—yasmin iti ||8||

**aṣṭāviṁśati-kṛtvovai vedo vyasto maharṣibhiḥ |**  
**vaivasvate’ntare tasmin dvāpareṣu punaḥ punaḥ ||9||**

**vedavyāsā vyatītā ye hy aṣṭāviṁśati sattama |**  
**caturdhā yaiḥ kṛto vedo dvāpareṣu punaḥ punaḥ ||10||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: aṣṭāviṁśatirvyāsā vyatītā nivṛttādhikārāḥ jātā ityarthaḥ | visargalopaśchāndasaḥ ||10|| 

**dvāpare prathamaḥ vyastaḥ svayaṁ vedaḥ svayambhuvā |**  
**dvitīye dvāpare caiva vedavyāsaḥ prajāpatiḥ ||11||**

**tṛtīye cośanā vyāsaś caturthe ca bṛhaspatiḥ |**  
**savitā pañcame vyāsaḥ ṣaṣṭhe mṛtyuḥ smṛtaḥ prabhuḥ ||12||**

**saptame ca tathaivendro vasiṣṭhaś cāṣṭame smṛtaḥ |**  
**sārasvataś ca navame tridhāmā daśame smṛtaḥ ||13||**

**ekādaśe tu triśikho bharadvājas tataḥ paraḥ |**  
**trayodaśecāntarikṣo varṇī cāpi caturdaśe ||14||**

**trayyāruṇaḥ pañcadaśe ṣoḍaśe tu dhanañjayaḥ |**  
**ṛtuñjayaḥ saptadaśe tad ūrdhvaṁ ca jayaḥ smṛtaḥ ||15||**

**tato vyāso bharadvājo bharadvājāc ca gautamaḥ |**  
**gautamād uttaro vyāso haryātmā yo’bhidhīyate ||16||**

**atha haryātmano’nte ca smṛto vājaśravā muniḥ |**  
**soma-śuṣmāyaṇas tasmāt tṛṇabindur iti smṛtaḥ ||17||**

**ṛkṣobhūd bhārgavas tasmād vālmīkir yo’bhidhīyate |**  
**tasmād asmat-pitā śaktir vyāsas tasmād ahaṁ mune ||18||**

**jātukarṇo’bhavan mattaḥ kṛṣṇa-dvaipāyanas tataḥ |**  
**aṣṭāviṁśatir ity ete vedavyāsāḥ purātanāḥ ||19||**

**eko vedaś caturdhā tu taiḥ kṛto dvāparādiṣu ||20||**

**bhaviṣye dvāpare cāpi drauṇir vyāso bhaviṣyati |**  
**vyatīte mama putre’smin kṛṣṇa-dvaipāyane mune ||21||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: prajāpatirmanuḥ— 

dvāpare tu purā vṛtte manoḥ svāyambhuve'ntare |   
brahmā manumuvācedaṁ vedān vyasya prajāpate || iti vāyūkteḥ | 

ita eva vacanād dvāparādiṣvityatra dvāpara ādiryeṣāṁ teṣu dvāparāṇāṁ sandhyāṁśeṣvityarthaḥ kalpyate | śāntanusamakāla satyavatyāṁ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanotpattiprasiddheḥ ||11-21||

**dhruvam ekākṣaraṁ brahma om ity eva vyavasthitam |**  
**bṛhatvād bṛṁhaṇatvāc ca tad brahmety abhidhīyate ||22||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: idānīṁ vedavibhāgaṁ vakṣyamāṇaḥ prathamaṁ tāvat praṇavāvacchinnabrahmaṇo vedāvirbhāvaṁ darśayitum āha—dhruvam iti | dhruvaṁ vedādīnāṁ prakṛtibhūtaṁ omityevaṁrūpaṁ vyavasthitamekamakṣaraṁ brahmetyabhidhīyate | tatra hetum āha—bṛhattvāt aparicchinna rūpabrahmātmakatvāt, bṛṁhaṇatvāt vedādīnāṁ kāraṇatvāt āvirbhāvakartṛtvāditi yāvat | yasmāduccāryamāṇa eva bṛṁhati bṛṁhayati tasmāducyate parabrahma' iti śruteḥ, omityekākṣaraṁ brahmeti gītokteśca ||22||

**praṇavāvasthitaṁ nityaṁ bhūr bhuvaḥ svar itīryate |**  
**ṛg-yajuḥ-sāmārtharvāṇo yat tasmai brahmaṇe namaḥ ||23||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tasyaiva vyāpakatvaṁ pratipādayan brahmaprakāśakatvaṁ brahmatvena prakāśatvaṁ brahmatvenopāsyaṁ praṇamati praṇaveti | bhūrbhuvaḥsvariti vyāhṛtitrayaṁ nityaṁ praṇavāvasthitamīryyate | tena vyāhṛtitrayātmakaṁ yadityarthaḥ | ṛgyajuḥsāmārthavāṇam iti prathamārthe dvitīyā | etadvedacatuṣṭayātmakañca yat tasmai brahmaṇe praṇavākhyāya nama iti ||23||

**jagataḥ pralayotpattyor yat tat kāraṇa-saṁjñitam |**  
**mahataḥ paramaṁ guhyaṁ tasmai subrahmaṇe namaḥ ||24||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: evaṁ vācakapraṇavapraṇāmānantaraṁ tadvācyaṁ brahma praṇamati jagata iti sārddhaistribhiḥ | jagataḥ pralayotpattyoḥ yat kāraṇasaṁjñitaṁ mahataśca paramaṁ guhyaṁ mukhyaṁ kāraṇaṁ tasmai subrahmaṇe pūjitaguṇādhiṣṭhātre brahmaṇe nama ityanvayaḥ ||24||

**agādhāpāram akṣayyaṁ jagat sammohanālayam |**  
**sva-prakāśa-pravṛttibhyāṁ puruṣārtha-prayojanam ||25||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tadeva viśinaṣṭi—agādhaṁ pūrvaparakālāvadhirahitam, apāraṁ sarvagatam, akṣayyaṁ kṣayitumaśakyaṁ, jagataḥ sammohanaṁ tamoguṇaḥ tasyāyamālayaḥ | kiñca samprakāśapravṛttibhyāṁ sattvarajoguṇābhyāṁ puruṣasya yo'rtho bhogāpavargalakṣaṇaḥ sa prayojanaṁ kāryaṁ yasya tat ||25||

**sāṅkhya-jñānavatāṁ niṣṭhā gatiḥ śama-damātmanām |**  
**yat tad avyaktam amṛtaṁ pravṛtti-brahma śāśvatam ||26||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tadevāha—sāṁkhyajñānaṁ pañcaviṁśatitattvajñānaṁ tadvatāṁ niṣṭhā prāpyaṁ sthānam | śamaḥ antaḥkaraṇavyāpāroparamaḥ, damaḥ bāhyendriyavyāpāroparamaḥ, sa eva ātmā svabhāvo yeṣāṁ teṣāṁ gatiḥ ātmānātmavivekakāraṇaṁ yattadavyaktamatīndriyam amṛtaṁ avināśi, pravṛttaṁ brahmapariṇāmavad brahma śāśvataṁ vastutaḥ sadaikarūpatayā vartamānam ||26||

**pradhānam ātma-yoniś ca guhā-saṁsthaṁ ca śabdyate |**  
**avibhāgaṁ tathā śukram akṣayaṁ bahudhātmakam ||27||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: pradhānaṁ mahadādikāryakartṛtvena pratīyamānam | yadvā pradhīyate adhīyate viśvamiheti pradhānam, ātmayoniḥ ananyakāryaṁ svataḥ siddham iti yāvat | guhāyāṁ hṛdayakuhare prakāśamānaṁ sattvaṁ yasya tat śasyate vedādiṣu | avirbhāgaḥ nirbhedam puṁstvamārṣam | śuklaṁ dīptimat svayamprabham iti yāvat | akṣaraṁ apakṣayaśūnyam | bahudhātmakam ||27||

**parama-brahmaṇe tasmai nityam eva namo namaḥ |**  
**yad rūpaṁ vāsudevasya paramātma-svarūpiṇaḥ ||28||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: yadevambhūtaṁ tathāpi paramabrahmaṇe kūṭasthaparipūrṇāya tasmai praṇavagamyāya nityaṁ namo nama iti bhaktyatiśayo dyotyate ||28||

**etad brahma tridhā bhedam abhedam api sa prabhuḥ |**  
**sarva-bhedeṣv abhedo’sau bhidyate bhinna-buddhibhiḥ ||29||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: idānīṁ vācyavācakapraṇavabrahmaṇa eva abhedavivakṣayā vyāhṛtyādirūpatām āha—yadrūpam iti sārddhaistribhiḥ | vāsudevasya yat praṇavākhyaṁ rūpametadabhedamapi tridhā vyāhṛtirūpeṇa bhūrādilokatrayarūpeṇa ca bhedo yasya tat | tatra hetumāha sa prabhuḥ praṇavātmā vāsudeva eva vibhinnābhirbuddhibhiḥ bhidyate bhinnatayā pratīyate | dṛśyate bhinnabuddhibhiriti pāṭhe viṣamadṛṣṭibhiḥ sarvabhūteṣvabhedo'sau dṛśyate ataḥ bhedamapi tatsvarūpam | tridhā bhidyate iti tridhā bhedaṁ jñānātmabhinnaṁ tridhā bhinnantu bhūrādyātmanetyarthaḥ ||29||

**sa ṛṅmayaḥ sāma-mayaḥ sarvātmā sa yajur-mayaḥ |**  
**ṛg-yajuḥ-sāmasārātmā sa evātmā śarīriṇām ||30||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: kiñca ṛgādimayaḥ ṛgvedādirūpaḥ ṛgādisāraḥ praṇavastadātmā ca śarīriṇāṁ vedavibhāgakartṛṇāmātmā ca sa eva ||30||

**na[^29] bhidyate vedamayaḥ sva-vedaṁ**  
**karoti bhedair bahubhiḥ saśākham |**  
**śākhā-praṇetā sa samasta-śākhā-**  
**jñāna-svarūpo bhagavān asaṅgaḥ ||31||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: praṇavākhyavāsudevasya sarvātmatvaṁ nivedayati—sa bhidyate iti | sa eva bhidyate ṛgādirūpeṇa bahubhirbhedaiḥ saśākham anekaprakārakaśākhākaṁ vedamātmānameva tattatpraṇetṛrūpaḥ san sa eva karoti sa eva samastaśākhārūpaśca | tatra hetubhūtaviśeṣaṇatrayam āha—jñānasvarūpo bhagavānananta iti | tena anantaśākhārūpatvaṁ tatpraṇetṛtvañcopapadyate iti ||30||

iti śrīdhara-kṛtāyām ātma-prakāśākhyāyāṁ svaprakāśākhyāyāṁ vā śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇa-ṭīkāyāṁ tṛtīyāṁ'śe tṛtīyo'dhyāyaḥ ||

|| iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe tṛtīyāṁśe tṛtīyo’dhyāyaḥ ||

—o)0(o—

(3.4)



## **veda-vyāsa-māhātmya-veda-vibhāga-varṇanaṁ** 

**parāśara uvāca—**  
**ādyo vedaś catuṣpādaḥ śata-sāhasra-sammitaḥ |**  
**tato daśa-guṇaḥ kṛtsno yajño’yaṁ sarva-kāma-dhuk ||1||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: aṣṭāviṁśe dvāpare'tra nānyatrāpi prasaṅgataḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanenaiva vedā vyastā itīryate | ādya īśvarād bhūtaścatuṣpāda ṛgādicaturbhedasamūharūpaḥ śatasāhasrasambhita ityarthaḥ | tataḥ pravṛtto'yaṁ kṛtsno jño daśaguṇaḥ daśavidhaḥ, agnihotradarśapaurṇamāsacāturmāsyapaśusomā iti pañcavidhaḥ, sa eva prakṛtivikṛtibhedena daśavidha iti | yadvā gṛhyoktaiḥ pañcayajñaiḥ saha daśavidhatvam ||1|| 

**tato’tra mat-suto vyāso[^30] aṣṭāviṁśatime’ntare |**  
**vedam ekaṁ catuṣpādaṁ caturdhā vyabhajat prabhuḥ ||2||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: atra manvantare aṣṭāviṁśatitame dvāpare catuṣpādamekaṁ santaṁ vedaṁ caturddhā ṛgyajuḥsāmātharvarūpeṇa pṛthag vyabhajata | prabhuḥ īśvaraḥ avatārarūpaḥ ||2||

**yathātra tena vai vyastā veda-vyāsena dhīmatā |**  
**vedas tathā samastais tair vyāsair anyais tathā mayā ||3||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: taiḥ pūrvaiḥ samastaiḥ mayā ca ṣaḍviṁśe vedā vyastāḥ ||3|| 

**tad anenaiva vyāsānāṁ śākhābhedān dvijottama |**  
**caturyugeṣu racitān samasteṣv avadhāraya ||4||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tat tasmāt anena kṛṣṇadvaipāyanakṛtena vedavibhāgena dṛṣṭāntena caturyugeṣu sarveṣvapi vedavibhāgān pūrvaiḥ kṛtān avadhāraya jānīhi ||4||

**kṛṣṇa-dvaipāyanaṁ vyāsaṁ viddhi nārāyaṇaṁ prabhum |**  
**ko’nyo hi bhuvi maitreya mahābhārata-kṛd bhavet ||5||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tadevaṁ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanavyāsasya mukhyatvamuktvā tatra hetum āha—kṛṣṇa iti | ataḥ asmin manvantara aṣṭāviṁśe eva dvāpare bhāratāvirbhāva iti gamyate ||5||

**tena vyastā yathā vedā mat-putreṇa mahātmanā |**  
**dvāpare hy atra maitreya tasmin śṛṇu yathātatham ||6||**

**brahmaṇā codito vyāso vedān vyastuṁ pracakrame |**  
**atha śiṣyān prajagrāha caturo veda-pāragān ||7||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vedapāragān vedasya pāraṁ gantuṁ samarthān ||7|| 

**ṛg-veda-pāṭhakaṁ pailaṁ jagrāha sa mahā-muniḥ |**  
**vaiśampāyana-nāmānaṁ yajur-vedasya cāgrahīt ||8||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: ṛgvedaśrāvakamiti-samāsasthamapi śrāvakapadamagre'nukṛṣya yojyaṁ pāragam iti kvacit pāṭhaḥ ||8||

**jaiminiṁ sāma-vedasya tathaivātharva-vedavit |**  
**sumantus tasya śiṣyo’bhūd vedavyāsasya dhīmataḥ ||9||**

**romaharṣaṇa-nāmānaṁ mahā-buddhiṁ mahā-muniḥ |**  
**sūtaṁ jagrāha śiṣyaṁ sa itihāsa-purāṇayoḥ ||10||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: itihāsapurāṇayoriti ārṣyādi bahudhākhyānaṁ devarṣicaritāśrayam | itihāsam iti proktaṁ bhaviṣyādbhutadharmayuk | sargādipañcalakṣaṇaṁ sargādyavatārabhedavivakṣayā daśalakṣaṇañca ||10||

**eka āsīd yajur-vedas taṁ caturdhā vyakalpayat |**  
**cāturhotram abhūt tasmiṁs tena yajñam athākarot ||11||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: eka āsīditi yajurvedikādhvaryavakriyābāhulyāt pradhānakarmaṇaśca yājanasya tadvihitatvāt yajuḥprādhānyādevamuktam— 

yacchiṣṭañca yajurveda tena yajñamayuñjata |   
yājanāddhi yajurveda iti śāstrasya niścayaḥ || iti vāyukteḥ |

hotropalakṣitāścatvāra ṛtvijaścatvāro hotāraḥ | taiḥ anuṣṭheyaṁ karma cāturhotram, tat yasminnabhūt, jātaṁ, tena caturddhā vibhaktena vedena yajñam akarot pravartitavān ||11|| 

**ādhvaravaṁ yajurbhis tu ṛgbhir hotraṁ tathā muniḥ |**  
**audgātraṁ sāmabhiś cakre brahmatvaṁ cāpy atharvabhiḥ ||12||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: cāturhotramevāha—ādhvaryavam iti ||12||

**tataḥ sa ṛca uddhṛtya ṛg-vedaṁ kṛtavān muniḥ |**  
**yajūṁṣi ca yajur-vedaṁ sāma-vedaṁ ca sāmabhiḥ ||13||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: caturdhā bhedam āha—tata iti | tataḥ vedarāśeḥ yajūṁṣyuddhṛtyetyanuṣaṅgaḥ | sāmabhirgītātmakairuddhṛtairityarthaḥ ||13|| 

**rājñāṁ cātharva-vedena sarva-karmāṇi ca prabhuḥ |**  
**kārayāmāsa maitreya brahmatvaṁ ca yathā-sthiti ||14||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: rājñaḥ sarvakarmāṇi śāntipuṣṭyādīni ||14|| 

**so’yam eko yathā vedas tarus tena pṛthak-kṛtaḥ |**  
**caturdhātha tato jātaṁ veda-pādapa-kānanam ||15||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: veda eva pādapāḥ tebhyaḥ kānanaṁ śākhā-praśākhāsantatiḥ eva kānanam iti vā ||15|| 

**bibheda prathamaṁ vipra pailo ṛgveda-pādapam |**  
**indra-pramitaye prādād bāṣkalāya ca saṁhite ||16||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: prathamaṁ ṛgvedapādapaṁ dvidhā vibheda ||16|| 

**caturdhā sa bibhedātha bāṣkalo’pi ca saṁhitām |**  
**bodhyādibhyo dadau tāś ca īcṣyebhyaḥ sa mahā-muniḥ ||17||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vāskala eva vāskaliḥ svārthe in ||17|| 

**bodhyāgnim āḍhakau tadvad yājñavalkya-parāśarau |**  
**pratiśākhās tu śākhāyās tasyās te jagṛhur mune ||18||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vāskalaye dattāyāḥ śākhāyā avāntaraśākhāste baudhyādayo jaguhuḥ ||18|| 

**indra-pramitir ekāṁ tu saṁhitāṁ sva-sutaṁ tataḥ |**  
**māṇḍukeyaṁ mahātmānaṁ maitreyādhyāpayat tadā ||19||**

**tasya śiṣya-praśiṣyebhyaḥ putra-śiṣya-kramād yayau ||20||**

**vedamitras tu śākalyaḥ saṁhitāṁ tām adhītavān |**  
**cakāra saṁhitāḥ pañca śiṣyebhyaḥ pradadau ca tāḥ ||21||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tasya pailaśiṣyasya indrapramateḥ śiṣyapraśiṣyebhyaḥ śiṣyapraśiṣyāṇāṁ putrān śiṣyāṁśca kramād yayau ||20-21||

**tasya śiṣyās tu ye pañca teṣāṁ nāmāni me śṛṇu |**  
**mudgalo gomukhaś caiva vātsyaḥ śālīya eva ca |**  
**śarīraḥ pañcamaś cāsīn maitreya sumahā-matiḥ ||22||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: bhedamitrākhyaḥ śākalya indrapramatisaṁhitām adhītavān | tataśca sa eva tasyāḥ pañca saṁhitāścakāra | tāśca śiṣyebhyaḥ mudgalādibhyo dadau ||22||

**saṁhitā-tritayaṁ cakre śāka-pūrṇas tathetaraḥ |**  
**niruktam akarot tadvac caturthaṁ muni-sattama ||23||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: śākapūrṇistu indrapramatiśiṣyastatsaṁhitāyāḥ saṁhitātritayaṁ niruktañca vedaśabdanirvacanarūpam akarot ||23|| 

**krauñco vaitālikas tadvad balākaś ca mahā-muniḥ |**  
**nirukta-kṛc caturtho’bhūd veda-vedāṅga-pāragaḥ ||24||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tacca saṁhitātritayaṁ krauñcādibhyaḥ adāt | caturtho niruktakṛt nāmeti kecit paṭhanti ||24||

**ity etāḥ pratiśākhābhyo hy anuśākhā dvijottama |**  
**bāṣkalaś cāparās tisraḥ saṁhitāḥ kṛtavān dvija |**  
**śiṣyaḥ kālāya-nirgārgyas tṛtīyaś ca kathājavaḥ ||25||**

**ity ete bahvṛcāḥ proktāḥ saṁhitā yaiḥ pravartitāḥ ||26||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: anuśākhāḥ avāntaraśākhāḥ | bāskaliḥ pailaśiṣyaḥ tisraḥ saṁhitāścake ityuktaṁ, sa evānyāstisraḥ saṁhitāḥ kṛtavān | apara eva śākalyasatīrtho bāskaliḥ tacchiṣyāḥ kālāyanipramukhāstrayaḥ ||26|| 

iti śrīdharakṛtāyāmātmaprakākhyāyāṁ vā svaprakāśākhyāyāṁ śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇa-ṭīkāyāṁ tṛtīyāṁ'śe caturtho'dhyāyaḥ ||

|| iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe tṛtīyāṁśe caturtho’dhyāyaḥ ||

—o)0(o—

(3.5)



## **yajur-veda-śākhā-vibhāgaḥ, yājñavalkya-kṛta-sūrya-stutiś ca** 

**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**  
**yajurveda-taroḥ śākhāḥ spatviṁśan mahāmuniḥ |**  
**vaiśampāyana-nāmāsau vyāsa-śiṣyaś cakāra vai ||1||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: pañcame'tha yajuḥśākhāḥ kathyante'tra samāsataḥ | setihāsaṁ taittirīyaṁ vājiśākhāpravarttanam || saptaviṁśat saptaviṁśatiḥ yajuṣaḥ pradhānaśākhāḥ | brahmāṇḍe tu ekādhikaśatamadhvaryuśākhā āpastamboktā uktāḥ ||1|| 

**śiṣyebhyaḥ pradadau tāś ca jagṛhus te’py anukramāt ||2||**

**yājñavalkyas tu tatrābhṛd brahmarāta-suto dvija |**  
**śiṣyaḥ parama-dharmajño guru-vṛtti-paraḥ sadā ||3||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: yajuḥśākhāntarāṇāmutpattiṁ vaktuṁ śiṣyāntaram āha—yājñavalkyastviti ||3|| 

**ṛṣir yo’dya mahā-meroḥ samāje nāgamiṣyati |**  
**tasya vai sapta-rātrāt tu brahma-hatyā bhaviṣyati ||4||**

**pūrvam evaṁ muni-gaṇaiḥ samayo yaḥ kṛto dvija |**  
**vaiśampāyana ekas tu taṁ vaytikrāntavāṁs tadā ||5||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tasmādeva śākhādvayapravṛttiṁ vaktuṁ itihāsam āha—ṛṣir iti | adya asmatsamāje ya ṛṣirnāgamiṣyati, tasyetaḥ saptarātrāt brahmahatyā bhaviṣyatīti yaḥ samayo'bhūt tat vaiśampāyana evātikrāntavāniti dvayoranvayaḥ ||5||

**svastrīyaṁ bālakaṁ so’tha padā spṛṣṭām aghātayat ||6||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: svatīyaṁ svasuḥ sutaṁ padā spṛṣṭaṁ santam aghātayat | ṛṣiśāpavaśāt padā spṛṣṭamātro'sau mamāretyarthaḥ ||6||

**śiṣyān āha sa bho śiṣyā brahma-hatyāpahaṁ vratam |**  
**caradhvaṁ mat-kṛte sarve na vicāryam idaṁ tathā ||7||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: samarthenānyena mahāpātake kṛte'nyena kathaṁ tatprāyaścitaṁ karttavyamitīdaṁ na vicārya, kintu tathā sākṣād vadhe śāstroktamukhyaprakāreṇa madarthaṁ vrataṁ caratetyarthaḥ ||7|| 

**athāha yājñavalkyas tu kim ebhir bhagavan dvijaiḥ |**  
**kleśitair alpatejobhiś cariṣye’ham idaṁ vratam ||8||**

**tataḥ kruddho guruḥ prāha yājñavalkyaṁ mahā-munim |**  
**mucyatāṁ yat tvayādhītaṁ matto viprāvamānaka ||9||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: viprāvamānaka viprāvamantaḥ ||9|| 

**nistejaso vadasy etān yat tvaṁ brāhmaṇa-puṅgavān |**  
**tena śiṣyeṇa nārtho’sti mamājñā-bhaṅga-kāriṇā ||10||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: sarvān śiṣyān pratyukte tanniṣidhya mayaiva kāryamityuktatvādājñābhaṅgakāriṇetyuktam ||10|| 

**yājñavalkyas tataḥ prāha bhaktyaitat te mayoditam |**  
**mamāpy alaṁ tvayādhītaṁ yan mayā tad idaṁ dvija ||11||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: mamāpi tvayā guruṇā alaṁ tvatto mayā yadadhītaṁ tadidam iti chardanamanucakāra ||11||

**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**  
**ity ukto rudhirāktāni sarūpāṇi yajūṁṣi saḥ |**  
**chardá dadau tasmai yayau sa svecchayā muniḥ ||12||**

**chardá dadau tasmai yayau sa svecchayā muniḥ |**  
**yajūṁṣy atha visṛṣṭāni yājñavalkyena vai dvija ||13||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: charditānāṁ sākṣād grahaṇamanucitam iti tittarāḥ pakṣiṇo bhūtvā jagṛhuḥ tato hetoste taittirīyāḥ prasiddhāḥ ||13|| 

**brahma-hatyā-vrataṁ cīrṇaṁ guruṇā coditais tu yaiḥ |**  
**carakādhvaryavas te tu caraṇān muni-sattama ||14||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: charditānāṁ sākṣād grahaṇamanucitam iti tittarāḥ pakṣiṇo bhūtvā jagṛhuḥ tato hetoste taittirīyāḥ prasiddhāḥ ||14|| 

**yājñavalkyo’pi maitreya prāṇāyāma-parāyaṇaḥ |**  
**tuṣṭāva prayataḥ sūryaṁ yajūṁṣy abhilaṣaṁs tataḥ ||15||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tato'sau sūryaṁ stutvā tatprasādāllabdhairyajurbhiḥ kāṇvādyāḥ pañcadaśa śākhāḥ kṛtavāniti darśayannāha—yājñavalkyo'pi ityādinā yāvadadhyāyasamāptiḥ ||15|| 

**yājñavalkya uvāca—**  
**namaḥ savitre dvārāya mukter amita-tejase |**  
**ṛg-yajuḥ-sāma-bhūtāya trayī-dhāmne ca te namaḥ ||16||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vimukteḥ dvārāya trayīdhāmavate trayīrūpatejaḥśāline ||16||

**namo’grīṣoma-bhūtāya jagataḥ kāraṇātmanā |**  
**bhāskarāya param tejaḥ-sauṣumna-ruci-vibhrate ||17||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: agnīsomabhūtāya ato jagataḥ kāraṇātmane | tadevāha—bhāskarāya ātapavṛṣṭidvārā jagatakāraṇatimi bhāvaḥ | tadupapādayati—tejo bibhrata ityagnirūpatvam | sauṣumnaṁ bibhrata iti somarūpatvam | uktañca sūryaraśmiḥ sauṣumno yastarpitastena candramā iti ||17||

**kalā-kāṣṭhā-nimeṣādi-kāla-jñānātma-rūpiṇe |**  
**dhyeyāya viṣṇu-rūpāya paramākṣara-rūpiṇe ||18||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: kalākāṣṭhādikālo jñāyate yena tathābhūtaḥ ātmā yasya tasmai dhyeyāya sarveṣāṁ dhyānārhāya, dhīmahi iti gāyatrīliṅgāt | paramākṣaraṁ brahma, akṣarāt parataḥ paraḥ | iti śruteḥ | tadrūpiṇe oṁkārarūpiṇe iti vā ||18||

**bibharti yaḥ sura-gaṇān āpyāyenduṁ sva-raśmibhiḥ |**  
**svadhāmṛtena ca pitṝṁs tasmai tṛpty-ātmanā namaḥ ||19||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: sudhāmṛtena sudhaiva amṛtam amaratvasādhanatvāt tena | tṛptyātmane tarpakāya | dhṛtātmana iti pāṭhe dhārayitre ||19|| 

**himāmbu-dharma-vṛṣṭīnāṁ kartā bhartā ca yaḥ prabhuḥ |**  
**tasmai trikāla-rūpāya namaḥ sūryāya vedhase ||20||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: himādīnāṁ yā vṛṣṭiḥ tatkartā | hemantavarṣāgrīṣmākhyatrikālarūpāya, vedhase sraṣṭre ||20||

**apahanti tamo yaś ca jagato’sya jagat-patiḥ |**  
**sattva-dhāma-dharo devo namas tasmaivivasvate ||21||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: sattvadhāmadharaḥ sattvamūrtidhara | satyadhāmadhara iti pāṭhe satyam avādhitaṁ dhāma tejo dharatīti pacādyac ||21||

**sat-karma-yogyo na jano naivāpaḥ śuddhi-kāraṇam |**  
**yasminn anudite tasmai namo devāya bhāsvate ||22||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: satkarma rātrisandhyetarakālavihitaṁ yat karma tadyogyaḥ ||22||

**spṛṣṭo yad aṁśubhir lokaḥ kriyā-yogyo hi jāyate |**  
**pavitratā-kāraṇāya tasmai śuddhātmanā namaḥ ||23||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: pūrvoktamevārthaṁ vidhimukhenāha spṛṣṭa iti ||23|| 

**namaḥ savitre sūryāya bhāskarāya vivasvate |**  
**ādityāyādi-bhūtāya devādīnāṁ namo namaḥ ||24||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: bhaktyatiśayena pūrvoktaiḥ paryāyaiḥ sarvaiḥ praṇamati—namaḥ savitre iti ||24|| 

**hiraṇmayaṁ rathaṁ yasya ketavo’mṛta-vājinaḥ |**  
**vahanti bhuvanāloki-cakṣuṣaṁ taṁ namāmy aham ||25||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: hiraṇmayaṁ tejomayam | ketavaḥ vedamayāḥ aśvā amṛtadhāyinaḥ amṛtāhārāḥ | udutyaṁ jātavedasam ityādi—ṛgartha uktaḥ | hiraṇmaye ratha iti pāṭhe ketavaḥ raśmayaḥ, amṛtaṁ jalaṁ taddhātāraḥ, vahanti gacchantītyarthaḥ ||25||

**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**  
**ity evam ādibhis tena stūyamānaḥ sa vai raviḥ |**  
**vāji-rūpa-dharaḥ prāha viryatām iti vāñchitam ||26||**

**yājñavalkyas tadā prāha praṇipatya divākaram |**  
**yajūṁṣi tāni me dehi yāni santi na me gurau ||27||**

**evam ukto dadau tasmai yajūṁṣi bhagavān raviḥ |**  
**ayāta-yāma-saṁjñāni yāni vetti na tad guruḥ ||28||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: ayātayāmasaṁjñāni anyairanabhyastāni ||28|| 

**yajūṁṣi yair adhītāni tāni viprair dvijottama |**  
**vājinas te samākhyātāḥ sūryo’py aśvo’bhavad yataḥ ||29||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vājinaḥ samākhyātāḥ vājirūpa—sūryaproktasaṁhitādhyāyitvādityarthaḥ ||28|| 

iti śrīdhara-kṛtāyām ātma-prakāśākhyāyāṁ svaprakāśākhyāyāṁ vā śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇa-ṭīkāyāṁ tṛtīyāṁ'śe pañcamo'dhyāyaḥ ||

**śākhā-bhedās tu teṣāṁ vai daśa pañca ca vājināṁ |**  
**kāṇvādyāḥ sumahābhāga yājñavalkyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||30||**

|| iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe tṛtīyāṁśe pañcamo’dhyāyaḥ ||

—o)0(o—

(3.6)



## **sāmātharva-veda-śākhā-vibhāgaḥ, purāṇa-nāma-lakṣaṇādi-nirūpaṇaṁ ca** 

**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**  
**sāma-veda-taroḥ śākhā vyāsa-śiṣyaḥ sa jaiminiḥ |**  
**krameṇa yena maitreya bibheda śṛṇu tan mama ||1||**

**sumantus tasya putro’bhūt sukarmāsyāpy abhūt sutaḥ |**  
**adhītavantau caikaikāṁ saṁhitāṁ tau mahā-matī ||2||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: sāmno'thātharvaṇaḥ śākhābhedāḥ paurāṇikā api | adhyetāraśca kartārasteṣāṁ ṣaṣṭhe nirūpitāḥ | tasya jaimineḥ | asya jaiminiputrasya sumanto | tau jaimine putrapautrau jaimininā vibhaktāmekaikāṁ saṁhitāṁ sva-svakāle'dhītavantau ||2|| 

**sahasra-saṁhitā-bhedaṁ sukarmā tat-sutas tataḥ |**  
**cakāra taṁ ca tac-chiṣyau jagṛhāte mahā-vratau ||3||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tatsutaḥ sumantusutaḥ tatsaṁhitābhedam ||3||

**hiraṇyanābhaḥ kausalyaḥ pauṣpiñjiś ca dvijottama |**  
**udīcyāḥ sāmagāḥ śiṣyās tasya pañcaśataṁ smṛtāḥ ||4||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: sukarmaṇaḥ śiṣyāvāha—hiraṇyanāma iti kauśalya iti hiraṇyanābhaviśeṣaṇam | ye pañcadaśa śiṣyāstebhyaḥ pañcadaśa saṁhitā hiraṇyanābhena dattāsta eva udīcyasāmagāḥ smṛtāḥ ||4||

**hiraṇyanābhāt tāvatyaḥ saṁhitā yair dvijottamaiḥ |**  
**gṛhītās te’pi cocyante paṇḍitaiḥ procya-sāmagāḥ ||5||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: yairaparairdvijottamaistāvatyasteṣāṁ grahītṛṇāṁ saṁkhyayā saṁkhyātāḥ saṁhitā hiraṇyanābhād gṛhītāḥ, te prācyasāmagā ucyanta ityanvayaḥ ||5|| 

**lokākṣir naudhamiś caiva kakṣīvān lāṅgalis tathā |**  
**pauṣpiñji-śiṣyās tad-bhedaiḥ saṁhitā bahulī-kṛtāḥ ||6||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: pauṣpiñjiśiṣyānāha—lokākṣir iti | tadbhedaiḥ tacchiṣyapraśiṣyādibhiḥ ||6||

**hiraṇyanābha-śiṣyas tu caturviṁśati-saṁhitāḥ |**  
**provāca kṛti-nāmāsau śiṣyebhyaś ca mahā-muniḥ ||7||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: hiraṇyanābhasya udīcyasāmagaśiṣyamadhye kṛtināmā śiṣyaḥ ||7|| 

**taiś cāpi sāmavedo’sau śākhābhir bahulīkṛtaḥ |**  
**atharvaṇāmatho vakṣye saṁhitānāṁ samuccayam ||8||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: taiḥ kṛtināmnaḥ śiṣyaiḥ ||8|| 

**atharva-vedaṁ sa muniḥ sumantur amita-dyutiḥ |**  
**śiṣyam adhyāpayāmāsa kabandhaṁ so’pi taṁ dvidhā ||9||**

**devadarśasya śiṣyās tu medho-brahmabalis tathā |**  
**śauklāyaniḥ pippalādas tathānyo dvija-sattama ||10||**

**pathyasyāpi trayaḥ śiṣyāḥ kṛtā yair dvija smaraṇāḥ |**  
**jābāliḥ kumudādiś ca tṛtīyaḥ śaunako dvija ||11||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: devadarśaḥ svasaṁhitāṁ caturdhā cakre | tāstu maud gādayaḥ catvāro jagṛhurityarthaḥ ||11|| 

**śaunakas tu dvidhā kṛtvā dadāv ekāṁ tu babhrave |**  
**dvitīyāṁ smaraṇāṁ prādāt saindhavāya ca saṁjñite ||12||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: pathyakṛtāstisraḥ saṁhitā jājalyādayo jagṛhuḥ, yai, svasaṁhitā bhinnā kṛtāḥ ||12||

**saindhavān muñjikeśaś ca dvedhābhinnās tridhā punaḥ |**  
**nakṣatra-kalpvedānāṁ saṁhitānāṁ tathaiva ca ||13||**

**caturthaḥ syād āṅgirasaḥ śāntikalpaś ca pañcamaḥ |**  
**śreṣṭhās tv atharvaṇām ete saṁhitānāṁ vikalpakāḥ ||14||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: saindhavāḥ saindhavāyanaśiṣyāḥ, muñjikeśā iti vabhroreva nāmāntaraṁ tacchiṣyā dvidhā dviprakārābhinnā vedāḥ sva sva saṁhitā yaiḥ te tathā | saṁhitābhedānāha—nakṣatrakalpa iti | vedānāṁ saṁhitānāñca kalpa ityanvayaḥ | tatra nakṣatrakalpo nakṣatrādipūjāvidhiḥ vedakalpo vaitālika brahmatvādibhiḥ saṁhitākalpaḥ saṁhitāvidhiḥ ||14||

**ākhyānaiś cāpy upākhyānair gāthābhiḥ kalpa-śuddhibhiḥ |**  
**purāṇa-saṁhitāṁ cakre purāṇārtha-viśāradaḥ ||15||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: āṅgirasakalpaḥ abhicārādividhiḥ śāntikalpaḥ aśva gajādyaṣṭādaśamahāśāntyādividhiḥ ||15||

**prakhyāto vyāsa-śiṣyo’bhūt sūto vai romaharṣaṇaḥ |**  
**purāṇa-saṁhitāṁ tasmai dadau vyāso mahā-matiḥ ||16||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: ākhyānādibhiḥ saha purāṇasaṁhitāñcakre vyāsa iti śeṣaḥ | tatra dṛṣṭopalabdhakathanamupākhyānaṁ pracakṣate, gāthā pitṛpṛthivyādigītāḥ, kalpasiddhiḥ vārāhādikalpanirṇayaḥ ||16||

**sumatiś cāgnivarcāś ca mitrāyuḥ śāṁsapāyanaḥ |**  
**akṛta-vraṇa-sāvarṇī ṣaṭ śiṣyās tasya cābhavan ||17||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: sumatyādayastasya romaharṣaṇasya ṣaṭ śiṣyāḥ tatkṛtāḥ ṣaṭ saṁhitā jagṛhuḥ ||17|| 

**kāśyapaḥ smaraṇā-kartā sāvarṇiḥ śāṁsapāyanaḥ |**  
**romaharṣaṇikā cānyā tisṝṇāṁ mūla-saṁhitā ||18||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: kāśyapādibhistribhiḥ kṛtāstisraḥ | akṛtavraṇa eva kāśyapaḥ kāśyapo'pyakṛtavraṇa iti vāyunoktaḥ | romaharṣaṇikā ca anyā romaharṣaṇena punaḥ saṁkṣepeṇa kṛtā ||18||

**catuṣṭayena bhedena saṁhitānāṁ idaṁ mune ||19||**

**ādyaṁ sarva-purāṇānāṁ purāṇaṁ brāhmam ucyate |**  
**aṣṭādaśa-purāṇāni purāṇa-jñāḥ pracaksāte ||20||**

**brāhmaṁ pādmaṁ vaiṣṇavaṁ ca śaivaṁ bhāgavataṁ tathā |**  
**tathānyaṁ nāradīyaṁ ca mārkaṇḍeyaṁ ca saptamam ||21||**

**āgneyam aṣṭamaṁ caiva bhaviṣyan navamaṁ smṛtam |**  
**daśamaṁ brahma-vaivartaṁ laiṅgam ekādaśaṁ smṛtam ||22||**

**vārāhaṁ dvādaśaṁ caiva skāndaṁ cātra trayodaśam |**  
**caturdaśaṁ vāmanaṁ ca kaurmaṁ pañcadaśaṁ tathā ||23||**

**mātsyaṁ ca gāruḍaṁ caiva brahmāṇḍaṁ ca tataḥ param |**  
**mahā-purāṇāny etāni hy aṣṭādaśa mahā-mune ||24||**

**tathā copapurāṇāny etāni munibhiḥ kathitāni ca |**  
**sargaś ca pratisargaś ca vaṁśa-manvantarāṇi ca |**  
**sarveṣv eteṣu kathyante vaṁśānucaritaṁ ca yat ||25||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: etāsāṁ saṁhitānāṁ catuṣṭayena sāroddhārarūpamidaṁ viṣṇupurāṇaṁ mune\! maitreya\! mayā kṛtam iti śeṣaḥ |

vyāsakṛtāni aṣṭādaśapurāṇānyāha—ādyam iti sārdhaiścaturbhiḥ | kecit tu saṁhitānāṁ catuṣṭayena idamādyaṁ brāhmamucyate iti vadanti ||19-25||

**yad etat tava maitreya purāṇaṁ kathyate mayā |**  
**etad vaiṣṇava-saṁjñaṁ vai pādmasya samanantaram ||26||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: ukteṣvaṣṭādaśapurāṇeṣu kimetat purāṇaṁ tvayā kathyata ityāha—yadetaditi mayā yadetat tava kathyate, tadevānāgatākhyānena padmapurāṇānantaraṁ vyāsena kṛtamityarthaḥ | yathāha—mātsye, varāhakalpavṛttāntamadhikṛtya parāśaraḥ | yān prāha dharmānakhilāṁstaduktaṁ vaiṣṇavaṁ viduḥ | ityevameva brahmādikathitaṁ vyāsena nibaddhaṁ brahmapurāṇādi kathyate | viṣṇupurāṇañca kvacit daśasāhasraṁ kvacidaṣṭasāhasram ity-ādi vikalpe'pi atra ṣaṭ sāhasrameva vyākhyāyate ||26||

**sarge ca pratisarge ca vaṁśa-manvantarādiṣu |**  
**kathyate bhagavān viṣṇur aśeṣeṣv eva sattama ||27||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: asya vaiṣṇavasaṁjñāyāṁ hetum āha—sarge ca iti ||27|| 

**aṅgāni vedāś catvāro mīmāṁsā nyāya-vistaraḥ |**  
**purāṇaṁ dharma-śāstraṁ ca vidyā hy etāś caturdaśa ||28||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: purāṇānāṁ vedoparbṛṁhaṇatvena dharmavedataddhetutvāt dharmavidyāsthāneṣu caturdaśasvantarbhāvam āha—aṅgāni iti | aṅgāni śikṣākalpajyotiśchandoniruktavyākaraṇāni ṣaṭ | caturaścatvāraḥ | dharmaśāstraṁ manvādiproktasmṛtiśāstram ||28||

**āyur-vedo dhanur-vedo gāndharvaś caiva te trayaḥ |**  
**artha-śāstraṁ caturthaṁ tu vidyā hy aṣṭādaśaiva tāḥ ||29||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: kevalaṁ dṛṣṭārthavidyāsthānamāyurvedādicatuṣkaṁ bruvan dharmavidyāsthānaiḥ sahāṣṭādaśavidyāsthānānyāha—āyur iti | āyurvedo'ṣṭāṅgacikitsāśāstram dhanvantariproktam | dhanurvedo bhṛguproktacaturvidha āyudhasandhānamokṣādiviṣayaḥ | gāndharvavedo bharatamunipraṇīto nṛtyagītādiviṣayaḥ | arthaśāstraṁ vārhaspatyādinītiśāstram | pūrvoktāścaturdaśetyaṣṭādaśavidyā iti ||29|| 

**jñeyā brahmarṣayaḥ pūrvaṁ tebhyo devarṣayaḥ punaḥ |**  
**rājarṣayaḥ punas tebhya ṛṣi-prakṛtayas trayaḥ ||30||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vedaśākhaprasaṅgāt kartṛṇāmaṣṭarṣīṇāṁ medānāha—jñeyā iti ||30|| 

**iti śākhāḥ samākhyātāḥ śākhā bhedās tathaiva ca |**  
**kartāraś caiva śākhānāṁ bheda-hetus tathoditaḥ ||31||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: upasaṁharati—iti iti | prasaṁkhyātāḥ saṁkhyayā proktāḥ śākhābhedāśca nāma uktāḥ | bhedahetuḥ puruṣāṇāmalpaprajñatvādiḥ ||31||

**sarva-manvantareṣv evaṁ śākhā-bhedāḥ samāḥ smṛtāḥ |**  
**prājāpatyā śrutir nityā tad-vikalpās tv ime dvija ||32||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: śākhānāṁ puruṣapraṇītatvena vedasya pauruṣeyatvaṁ syādityata āha—prājāpatya iti kalpādau prajāpatinā dṛṣṭā śrutiḥ | nityaiva ime tu śākhābhedāstasyā eva vikalpaḥ, te grahaṇasaukaryārthamavāntarabhedāḥ, na tvapūrvāḥ puruṣaiḥ kṛtā ityarthaḥ ||32|| 

iti śrīdhara-kṛtāyām ātma-prakāśākhyāyāṁ svaprakāśākhyāyāṁ vā śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇa-ṭīkāyāṁ tṛtīyāṁ'śe ṣaṣṭho'dhyāyaḥ ||

**etat te kathitaṁ sarvaṁ yat pṛṣṭo’ham iha tvayā |**  
**maitreya veda-sambandhaḥ kim anyat kathayāmi te ||33||**

iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe tṛtīyāṁśe ṣaṣṭho’dhyāyaḥ

—o)0(o—

(3.7)



## **yama-gītā**

**śrī-maitreya uvāca—**  
**yathāvat kathitaṁ sarvaṁ yat pṛṣṭo’si mayā guro |**  
**śrotum icchāmy ahaṁ tv ekaṁ tad bhavān prabravītu me ||1||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vedaśākhāpraṇayanamuktaṁ kādibhedataḥ | atha tāntrikadharmaśca setihāso'tra varṇyate | bhūtalādiprasaṅgānuprasaṅgādanuvarṇyate | sadgatistatsthajantūnāṁ bhagavaddharmasaṅgataḥ | uktamabhinandan śrutismṛtisārabhūtaṁ dharmaṁ pṛcchati—yathāvad iti saptabhiḥ ||1|| 

**sapta dvīpāni pātāla-vidhayaś ca mahā-mune |**  
**sapta-lokāś ca ye’ntaḥ-sthā brahmāṇḍasyāsya sarvataḥ ||2||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: pātālavīthī bhūvivarapaṁktiḥ | sapta lokāḥ svargādayā | etat saptadvīpādirūpaṁ sarvam ||2||

**sthūlaiḥ sūkṣmais tathā sūkṣma-sūkṣmāt sūkṣmatarais tathā |**  
**sthūlāt sthūlataraiś caiva sarvaṁ prāṇibhir āvṛtam ||3||**

**aṅgulasyāṣṭa-bhāgo’pi na so’sti muni-sattama |**  
**na santi prāṇino yatra karma-bandha-nibandhanāḥ ||4||**

**sarve caite vaśaṁ yānti yamasya bhagavan kila |**  
**āyuṣo’nte tathā yānti yātanās tat pracoditāḥ ||5||**

**yātanābhyaḥ paribhraṣṭā devādyāsv atha yoniṣu |**  
**jantavaḥ parivartante śāstrāṇāṁ eṣa nirṇayaḥ ||6||**

**so’ham icchāmi tac chrotuṁ yamasya vaśa-vartinaḥ |**  
**na bhavanti narā yena tat karma kathayasva me ||7||**

**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**  
**ayam eva mune praśno nakulena mahātmanā |**  
**pṛṣṭaḥ pitāmahaḥ prāha bhīṣmo yat tac chṛṇuṣva me ||8||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: ayameva praśnaḥ praṣṭavyo'rtho nakulena bhīṣmaṁ prati pṛṣṭaḥ, tataśca sa bhīṣmastaṁ prati yat prāha tacca śṛṇuṣva ||8||

**bhīṣma uvāca—**  
**purā mamāgato vatsa sakhā kāliṅgako dvijaḥ |**  
**sa mām uvāca pṛṣṭo vai mayā jāti-smaro muniḥ ||9||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: sa kāliṅgako dvijo māmuvāca—mayā jātismaro muniḥ pṛṣṭa iti ||9|| 

**tenākhyātam idaṁ sarvam itthaṁ caitad bhaviṣyati |**  
**tathā ca tad abhūd vatsa yathoktaṁ tena dhīmatā ||10||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tena jātismareṇa idamidaṁ vartamānametaditthamevaṁlakṣaṇaṁ bhaviṣyatīti ca kāliṅgasthāne yadākhyātaṁ, tena ca kāliṅgakena mahyaṁ yathoktaṁ, tathaivaṁ tadabhūt, he vatsa nakuletyanvayaḥ ||10||

**sa pṛṣṭaś ca mayā bhūyaḥ śraddadhānena vai dvijaḥ |**  
**yad yad āha na tad dṛṣṭam anyathā hi mayā kvacit ||11||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: śraddadhānamanoyuktena sa kāliṅgako dvijo bhūyaḥ punaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ san jātismaravākyaṁ yadyadāha, tadanyathā vyabhicāri mayā na dṛṣṭamityativiśvāsārthamuktam ||11|| 

**ekadā tu mayā pṛṣṭam etad yad bhavatoditam |**  
**prāha kāliṅgako vipraḥ smṛtvā tasya muner vacaḥ ||12||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: prakṛtamāha ekada iti | tasya jātismarasya muneḥ ||12|| 

**jāti-smareṇa kathito rahasyaḥ paramo mama |**  
**yama-kiṅkarayor yo’bhūt saṁvādas taṁ bravīmi te ||13||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tadevāha—jāti iti | taṁ saṁvādaṁ saṁvādaviṣayārtham ||13|| 

**kāliṅga uvāca—**  
**kha-puruṣam abhivīkṣya pāśa-hastaṁ**  
**vadati yamaḥ kila tasya karṇa-mūle |**  
**parihara madhusūdana-prapannān**  
**prabhur aham anya-nṝṇām avaiṣṇavānām ||14||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tamevāha—svapuruṣam ityādibhiḥ so'nyalokya ityantairekaviṁśatyā ślokaiḥ | pāpijanānayanāya udyataṁ pāśahastaṁ svapuruṣamabhivīkṣya viṣṇubhaktān parityajyānyānānayeti svapratāpabhaṅgabhiyā atirahasyatayā ca karṇamūle vadati sma ||14||

**aham amarārcitena dhātrā**  
**yama iti loka-hitāhite niyuktaḥ |**  
**hari-guru-vaśago’smi na svatantraḥ**  
**prabhavati saṁyamane mamāpi viṣṇuḥ ||15||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: na vaiṣṇavānāṁ prabhurityatra hetum āha—aham iti | prajāsaṁyamanād yama iti saṁjñayā lokahitāhite śubhāśubhaphaladānārthe dhātrā niyukto'pi harireva gurustadvaśago'smi, na svatantraḥ | yato mamāpi saṁyamane daṇḍe viṣṇuḥ prabhavati | hitāya sa niyukta iti pāṭhe daṇḍo'pi pādakṣayārthatayā hita eva tasmādapi ||15||

**kaṭaka-mukuṭa-karṇikādi-bhedaiḥ**  
**kanakam abhedam apīṣyate yathaikam |**  
**sura-paśu-manujādi-kalpanābhir**  
**harir akhilābhir udīryate tathaikaḥ ||16||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tatra hetum āha—kaṭaka iti dvābhyām | sarvotpattipralayahetutvena sarvātmakatvāt sarvaniyantṛtvamityarthaḥ, kaṭako valayaḥ, karṇikā karṇabhūṣaṇam | kaṭakādibhedairnānārūpaiḥ kāryairupalakṣitamapi abhedaṁ kāraṇātmanā ekameveṣyane yathā, tathaika eva jagat kāraṇabhūto hariḥ surādibhedairudīryate ||16||

**kṣiti-tala-paramāṇavo’nilānte**  
**punar upayānti yathaikatāṁ dharitryāḥ |**  
**sura-paśu-manujādayas tathānte**  
**guṇa-kaluṣeṇa sanātanena tena ||17||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: kiñca bhedasya māyopādhikatvānmāyānāśe tu viṣṇureka eva ityāha—kṣiti iti | anilodravṛtāḥ kṣitijalaparamāṇavo yathā anilasyānte avasāne dharitryādinā sahaikatāṁ yānti tathā guṇānāṁ kaluṣeṇa kāluṣyeṇa kṣobheṇa ye surādayo jātāḥ ante guṇakṣobhoparame tena viṣṇunā sahaikatāṁ yāntītyanvayaḥ ||17||

**harim amara-gaṇārcitāṅghri-padmaṁ**  
**praṇamati yaḥ paramārthato hi martyaḥ |**  
**tam apagata-samasta-pāpa-bandhaṁ**  
**vraja parihṛtya yathāgnim ājya-siktam ||18||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tarhi yamasyāpi niyanturbhaktiḥ kathaṁ manuṣyasādhayetyata āha—harim iti | paramārthataḥ sarvātmatvena hariṁ yaḥ praṇamatyapi taṁ parityajya vraja | yadvā haripraṇatimātreṇa paramārthataḥ tamapagatasamastapāpabandhamityanvayaḥ | anena dṛṣṭāntena bhaktasaṁsargiṇo'pi tyājyā ityuktaṁ, ye'nye ca pāpāḥ padamāśrayāśrayāḥ śudhyanti iti śukokteḥ ||18||

**iti yama-vacanaṁ niśamya pāśī**  
**yama-puruṣas tam uvāca dharma-rājam |**  
**kathaya mama vibho samasta-dhātur**  
**bhavati hareḥ khalu yādṛśo’sya bhaktaḥ ||19||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: samastasya dhātuḥ pālakasya ||19||

**yama uvāca—**  
**na calati nija-varṇa-dharmato yaḥ**   
**sama-matir ātma-suhṛd-vipakṣa-pakṣe |**  
**na harati na hanti kiñcid uccaiḥ**   
**sthita-manasaṁ tam avehi viṣṇu-bhaktam ||20||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: na haratīti yaduktaṁ tadviśeṣam āha—kanakam iti | kanakamapi rahasyāpi dṛṣṭvā parasvaṁ tṛṇamiva yaḥ samavaiti jighṛkṣāvimukho bhavatītyarthaḥ | atha ca bhagavati ananyacetāḥ bhavati tam ||22||

**kali-kaluṣa-malena yasya nātmā**  
**vimalamater malinīkṛtas tam enam |**  
**manasi kṛta-janārdanaṁ manuṣyaṁ**  
**satatam avehi harer atīva-bhaktam ||21||**

**kanakam api rahasy avekṣya buddhyā**  
**tṛṇam iva yaḥ samavaiti para-svam |**  
**bhavati ca bhagavaty ananya-cetāḥ**   
**puruṣa-varaṁ tam avehi viṣṇu-bhaktam ||22||**

**sphaṭika-giri-śilāmalaḥ kva viṣṇur**  
**manasi nṝṇāṁ kva ca matsarādi-doṣaḥ |**  
**na hi tuhina-mayūkha-raśmi-puñje**  
**bhavati hutāśana-dīptijaḥ pratāpaḥ ||23||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: sitamanasam iti viśeṣaṇaṁ yaduktaṁ tadeva kvaśabdābhyāṁ spaṣṭayati—sphaṭika iti | sphaṭikagiriśileva amalaḥ tuhinamayūkhaścandrastasya raśmipuñje matsarādidoṣasya viṣṇubhakteśca virodhoktyā taddoṣarahitasyaiva viṣṇubhaktatvamityuktaṁ bhavati ||23||

**vimala-matir amatsaraḥ praśāntaḥ**   
**śuci-carito’khila-sattva-mitra-bhūtaḥ |**  
**priya-hita-vacano’stumānamāyo**  
**vasati sadā hṛdi tasya vāsudevaḥ ||24||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tadeva vidhimukhena vivṛṇoti—vimalamatir iti | śuci śuddhaṁ caritaṁ yasya, akhilānāṁ sattvānāṁ mitrabhūtaḥ, aste niraste mānamāye garvālīke yena saḥ ||24||

**vasati hṛdi sanātane ca tasmin**  
**bhavati pumān jagato’sya saukhya-rūpaḥ |**  
**kṣiti-rasam atiramyam ātmano’ntaḥ**  
**kathayati cārutayaiva śālapotaḥ ||25||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tasya prasannataiva cihnamityāha—vasati iti | uktamarthamarthāntaranyāsena samarthayati—kṣitirasam iti | śālapoto bālaḥ śālataruḥ cārutayā sukumāratayaiva ramyaṁ kṣitirasaṁ svasyāntaryathā kathayati anumāpayati, evaṁ sarvabhūteṣu saumyatayā viṣṇubhakto'pi viṣṇuṁ hṛdi vasantaṁ sūcayatītyarthaḥ ||25||

**yama-niyama-vidhūta-kalmaṣāṇām**  
**anudinam acyuta-sakta-mānasānām |**  
**apagatam adamāna-matsarāṇāṁ**  
**vraja bhaṭa dūratareṇa mānavānām ||26||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: kiñca yamaniyama iti ahiṁsāsatyāsteyabrahmacaryāparigrahā yamāḥ, śaucasantoṣatapaḥ svādhyāyeśvarapraṇidhānāni niyamāḥ, dhanādisampatsamutsikto manasa ullāso madaḥ, ātmani pūjyatābuddhirmānaḥ, paraśubhadveṣo matsaraḥ ||26||

**hṛdi yadi bhagavān anādir āste**  
**harir asi-śaṅkha-gadādharo’vyayātmā |**  
**tad agham agha-vighāta-kartṛ-bhinnaṁ**  
**bhavati kathaṁ sati cāndhakāram arke ||27||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: apagatakalmaṣatvamevāha hṛdi iti | asisthāne apīti kvacit pāṭhaḥ | tat tarhi aghānāṁ vighātakartā haristena bhinnaṁ nāśitaṁ sadaghaṁ kathaṁ bhavati balavadvirodhina sati aparaṁ na tiṣṭhatītyarthāntareṇa spaṣṭayati—katham iti ||27|| 

**harati para-dhanaṁ nihanti jantūn**   
**vadati tathānṛta-niṣṭhurāṇi yaś ca |**  
**aśubha-janita-durmadasya puṁsaḥ**   
**kaluṣa-mater hṛdi tasya nāsty anantaḥ ||28||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: idānīmabhaktalakṣaṇānyāha—harati iti caturbhiḥ ||28||

**na sahati para-sampadaṁ vinindāṁ**  
**kaluṣa-matiḥ kurute satām asādhuḥ |**  
**na yajati na dadāti yaś ca santaṁ**  
**manasi na tasya janārdano’dhamasya ||29||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: satāṁ vinindāṁ kurute, santamarthaṁ na dadāti | yadvā santaṁ viṣṇuṁ tadbhaktaṁ vā na yajati na pūjayati, na ca tasmai dadāti ||29||

**parama-suhṛdi bāndhave kalatre**  
**suta-tanayā-pitṛ-mātṛ-bhṛtya-varge |**  
**śaṭha-matir upayāti yo’rtha-tṛṣṇāṁ**  
**tam adhama-ceṣṭam avehi nāsya bhaktam ||30||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: paramasuhṛdādiṣu śaṭhamatiḥ sannarthatṛṣṇāṁ karoti, arthāt tebhya evārthaṁ grahītuṁ vāñchati | yadvā paramasuhṛdādau teṣāṁ nimittamanyāyenāpyarthatṛṣṇāṁ karoti ||30||

**aśubha-matir asat-pravṛtti-saktaḥ**  
**satatam anārya-kuśīla-saṅga-mattaḥ |**  
**anudina-kṛta-pāpa-bandha-yuktaḥ**  
**puruṣa-paśur na hi vāsudeva-bhaktaḥ ||31||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: anāryaiḥ viśālo dīrghakālo yaḥ saṅgastena mattaḥ | anāryakuśīleti pāṭhe nīcaiḥ duḥśīlaiśca yaḥ saṅgastena mattaḥ ityarthaḥ ||31||

**sakalam idam ahaṁ ca vāsudevaḥ**  
**parama-pumān parameśvaraḥ sa ekaḥ |**  
**iti matir acalā bhavaty anante**  
**hṛdaya-gate vraja tān vihāya dūrāt ||32||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: uktamabhaktacihnaṁ bhaktacihnamāha sakalam iti ||32|| 

**kamala-nayana vāsudeva viṣṇo**  
**dharaṇidharācyuta śaṅkha-cakra-pāṇe |**  
**bhava śaraṇam itīrayanti ye vai**  
**tyaja bhaṭa dūratareṇa tān apāpān ||33||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tannāmakīrttanaṁ tadekaśaraṇatā caikāntabhaktacihnamityāha kamalanayana iti ||33||

**vasati manasi yasya so’vyayātmā |**  
**puruṣa-varasya na tasya dṛṣṭi-pāte |**  
**tava gatir atha vā mamāsti cakra-**  
**pratihata-vīrya-balasya so’nya-lokyaḥ ||34||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: dūratareṇa tyajeti yaduktaṁ tatrahetumāha vasatīti | tasya dṛṣṭipātaṁ yāvaccakrabhramaṇādatastaccakreṇa pratihate vīryabale yasya tasya tava mama ca tadṛṣṭipātaviṣaye pāpijanānayane'pi na gatirasti sa punaranyalokyaḥ vaikuṇṭhavāsārhaḥ nāsmalloka yogyaḥ ||34|| 

**kāliṅga uvāca—**  
**iti nija-bhaṭa-śāsanāya devo**  
**ravi-tanayaḥ sa kilāha dharma-rājaḥ |**  
**mama kathitam idaṁ ca tena tubhyaṁ**  
**kuru-vara samyag idaṁ mayāpi coktam ||35||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: mama mahyaṁ, tena jātismaraṇena, karuvara\! he bhīṣma ||35|| 

**śrī-bhīṣma uvāca—**  
**nakulaitan mamākhyātaṁ pūrvaṁ tena dvijanmanā |**  
**kaliṅga-deśād abhyetya prītena sumahātmanā ||36||**

**mayāpy etad yathā-nyāyaṁ samyag vatsa tavoditam |**  
**yathā viṣṇum ṛte nānyat trāṇaṁ saṁsāra-sāgare ||37||**

**kiṅkarāḥ pāśa-daṇḍāś ca na yamo na ca yātanāḥ |**  
**samarthās tasya yasyātmā keśavālambanaḥ sadā ||38||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tasya vaśīkartuṁ na samarthāḥ | keśavālambanaḥ keśavāśrayaḥ ||38|| 

iti śrīdhara-svāmi-kṛtāyām ātma-prakāśākhyāyāṁ svaprakāśākhyāyāṁ vā śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇa-ṭīkāyāṁ tṛtīyāṁ'śe saptamo'dhyāyaḥ

**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**  
**etan mune samākhyātaṁ gītaṁ vaivasvatena yat |**  
**tvat-praśnānugataṁ samyak kim anyac chrotum icchasi ||39||**

iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe tṛtīyāṁśe saptamo’dhyāyaḥ

—o)0(o—

(3.8)



## **śrī-viṣṇu-pūjāyāṁ phala-śrutiḥ, cāturvarṇya-dharma-kathanaṁ ca**

**śrī-maitreya uvāca—**  
**bhagavan bhagavān devaḥ saṁsāra-vijigīṣubhiḥ |**  
**samākhyāhi jagannātho viṣṇur ārādhyate yathā ||1||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: viṣṇorārādhanopāyo nijadharmaprasaṅgataḥ | sagaraurvīyasaṁvādaṁ navādhyāyairnirūpyate | yathā yatprakāreṇa dharmeṇa ||1|| 

**ārādhitāc ca govindād ārādhana-parair naraiḥ |**  
**yat prāpyate phalaṁ śrotuṁ tac cecchāmi mahā-mune ||2||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: viṣṇorārādhanaparairājñānuṣṭhānatatparaiḥ ||2|| 

**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**  
**yat pṛcchati bhavān etat sagareṇa mahātmanā |**  
**aurvaḥ prāha yathā pṛṣṭas tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu ||3||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: svargibandhaṁ brahmalokādipadam ||3|| 

**sagaraḥ praṇipatyainam aurvaṁ papraccha bhārgavam |**  
**viṣṇor ārādhanopāya-sambandhaṁ muni-sattama ||4||**

**phalaṁ cārādhite viṣṇau yat puṁsām abhijāyate |**  
**sa cāha pṛṣṭo yatnena tasmai tan me’khilaṁ śṛṇu ||5||**

**aurva uvāca—**  
**bhaumaṁ manorathaṁ svargaṁ svarge ramyaṁ ca yat padam |**  
**prāpnoty ārādhite viṣṇau nirvāṇam api cottamam ||6||**

**yad yad icchati yāvac ca phalam ārādhite’cyute |**  
**tat tad āpnoti rājendra bhūri svalpam athāpi vā ||7||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: yāvat yatsaṁkhyakaṁ bhūri svalpaṁ veti pramāṇataḥ ||7||

**yat tu pṛcchasi bhūpāla katham ārādhyate hariḥ |**  
**tad ahaṁ sakalaṁ tubhyaṁ kathayāmi nibodha me ||8||**

**varṇāśramācaravatā puruṣeṇa paraḥ pumān |**  
**viṣṇur ārādhyate panthā nānyat tat-toṣa-kāraṇam ||9||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: varṇāśramācāravatety-adhikāri-viśeṣaṇād vedokta-tad-aviruddha-purāṇāgamādy-uktācāravān eva tatrādhikārī, na vigītācāraḥ | anyaḥ śruty-ukta-dharma-parityāgena tad-vrata-dhāraṇa-śravaṇa-kīrtanādi-rūpaḥ panthā na bhavati ||9||

**digdarśinī** (bṛ.bhā. 6.204): **varṇāśramācāraḥ** svadharmas **tadvatā puruṣeṇa viṣṇur ārādhyata** eva, **na cānyat** kiñcit sādhyate nāpi tenaiva kṛta-kṛtyatayā sarvata uparamyata ity arthaḥ | evaṁ varṇāśramācārāṇāṁ viṣṇor ārādhanam eva phalam iti paryavasitam | kutaḥ ? anya ārādhanāt **paraḥ** panthāḥ karma-jñānādi-mārgas **tasya** viṣṇos **toṣa-kāraṇaṁ** na syāt | no cet svātantryeṇa teṣāṁ tat-toṣa-kāraṇatvāyogyatvād bhakty-anusaraṇaṁ vinā vaiyārthyāpattir eva syāt iti | atas tad-vacanaṁ—

śruti-smṛtī mamaivājñe yas te ullaṅghya vartate |   
ājñā-cchedī mama drohī mad-bhakto'pi na vaiṣṇavaḥ || \[?\] ity-ādikam |

anyam api tādṛśaṁ varṇāśramācārāṇāṁ bhakti-pravṛtti-hetutvena prathamaṁ parityāgāyogyatvāt sarvathā tat-tyāga-nirasanārthakaṁ | kiṁ vā, pravṛtti-paraveda-mārga-rakṣārthakaṁ kiṁ vā, bhakti-viṣayakāpekṣā-śraddhā-viśeṣa-rahita-jana-viṣayakam iti boddhavyam | sarvatraiva karmaṇāṁ sāvadhitvādi-śravaṇād-bhakti-parāṇāṁ karmādi-lopenāpi pātity-ādi-doṣānutpatteḥ | tad uktaṁ śrī-bhagavataiva padma-purāṇe—

mat-karma kurvatāṁ puṁsāṁ kriyā-lopo bhaved yadi |   
teṣāṁ karmāṇi kurvanti tisraḥ koṭyo maharṣayaḥ || iti | 

tathā tatraiva devadyuti-stutau—

yasmin jñāte na kurvanti karma caiva śrutīritam |   
nireṣaṇā jaganmitrāḥ śuddhaṁ brahma namāmi tam || iti | 

jñāte'pi kiṁ vaktavyam ? āśrite sevite vā satīti tathaikādaśa-skandhe'pi—

tāvat karmāṇi kurvīta na nividyeta yāvatā |   
mat-kathā-śravaṇādau vā śraddhā yāvan na jāyate || \[bhā.pu. 11.20.9\] iti | 

*karmāṇi* nitya-naimittikāni | vā-śabdo'trānya-nirapekṣatayā asya pakṣasya vaiśiṣṭyaṁ sūcayati—

mahāntas te sama-cittāḥ praśāntā vimanyavaḥ suhṛdaḥ sādhavo ye |   
ye vā mayīśe kṛta-sauhṛdārthāḥ \[bhā.pu. 5.5.2-3\] itivat | 

śraddhā viśvāsaḥ | kiṁ ca, 

na mayy ekānta-bhaktānāṁ guṇa-doṣodbhavā guṇāḥ |   
sādhūnāṁ sama-cittānāṁ buddheḥ param upeyuṣām || \[bhā.pu. 11.20.36 \] iti | 

guṇa-doṣair vihita-pratiṣiddhair udbhavo yeṣāṁ te guṇāḥ pūṇya-pāpādaya iti | śrī-śivenāpi—

smartavyaḥ satataṁ viṣṇur vismartavyo na jātucit |   
sarve vidhi-niṣedhāḥ syur etayor eva kiṅkarāḥ || iti | 

asyārthaḥ—*kadācid api na* *vismartavyaḥ* | *etayoḥ* smaraṇa-vismaraṇayor eva *kiṅkarāḥ* adhīnāḥ | smṛtāv eva sarva-vidhayaḥ tat-kṛtāśeṣa-puṇyāni, vismṛtāv eva sarve niṣedhāḥ tat-kṛtāśeṣa-pāpāni bhavantīti | atas tatraiva yatnaḥ kāryaḥ, na cānyatra iti bhāvaḥ ||9||

**yajan yajñān yajaty enaṁ japaty enaṁ japan nṛpa |**  
**nighnann anyān hinasty enaṁ sarva-bhūto yato hariḥ ||10||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: yajñān yaṣṭavyān indrādīn yajan viṣṇuṁ yajati, yaṁ kañcana japan viṣṇumeva japati, anyaṁ ghnan viṣṇumeva hanti ||10||

**tasmāt sadācāravatā puruṣeṇa janārdanaḥ |**  
**ārādhyate sva-varṇokta-dharmānuṣṭhāna-kāriṇā ||11||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: yataḥ pūjya vadhyādisarvasvarūpo viṣṇustasmāt tadājñayā varṇāśramadharmān yāgādīn sadācārāṁśca kurvatā viṣṇurārādhyate toṣyate | sadācāraḥ avigītaśiṣṭācāraḥ ||11|| 

**brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriy vaiśyaḥ śūdraś ca pṛthivī-pate |**  
**sva-dharma-tatparo viṣṇum ārādhayati nānyathā ||12||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: uktamarthamevādhikāridarśanapūrvakaṁ vyatirekamukhena draḍhayati—brāhmaṇa iti ||12|| 

**parāpavādaṁ paiśunhyam anṛtaṁ ca na bhāṣate |**  
**anyodvega-karaṁ vāpi toṣyate tena keśavaḥ ||13||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tatra sādhāraṇadharmānāha ṣaḍbhiḥ | parasyāpavāḍhaṁ samakṣanindāṁ, paiśunyaṁ parokṣe rahodoṣakathanam ||13|| 

**para-patnī-para-dravya-para-hiṁsāsu yo matim |**  
**na karoti pumān bhūpa toṣyate tena keśavaḥ ||14||**

**yo manuṣyo manuṣyendra toṣyate tena keśavaḥ ||15||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: na hanti na prāṇān viyojayati | prāṇino jaṅgamānanyān dehinaḥ sthāvarān | eteṣāṁ niyamenākriyamāṇānāṁ dharmatvena haritoṣaṇatvāccittaśodhakatvam ||15||

**deva-dvija-gurūṇāṁ ca śuśrūṣāsu sadodyataḥ |**  
**na tāḍayati no hanti prāṇino’nyāṁś ca dehinaḥ |**  
**toṣyate tena govindaḥ puruṣeṇa nareśvara ||16||**

**yathātmani ca putre ca sarva-bhūteṣu yas tathā |**  
**hita-kāmo haris tena sarvadā toṣyate sukham ||17||**

**yasya rāgādi-doṣeṇa na duṣṭaṁ nṛpa mānasam |**  
**viśuddha-cetasā viṣṇus toṣyate tena sarvadā ||18||**

**varṇāśrameṣu ye dharmāḥ śāstroktā nṛpa-sattama |**  
**teṣu tiṣṭhan naro viṣṇum ārādhayati nānyathā ||19||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: idānīṁ haritoṣakān sādhāraṇadharmānāha—varṇa iti | tiṣṭhanniti hetau śatṛpratyayaḥ | teṣu sthitistadanuṣṭhānanārādhanaheturityarthaḥ ||19||

**sagara uvāca—**  
**tad ahaṁ śrotum icchāmi varṇa-dharmān aśeṣataḥ |**  
**tathaivāśrama-dharmāṁś ca dvija-varya bravīhi tān ||20||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tat tarhi tān śrotumicchāmi, bravīhītyarthaḥ ||20||

**aurva uvāca—**  
**brāhmaṇa-kṣatriya-viśāṁ śūdrāṇāṁ ca yathā-kramam |**  
**tvam ekāgra-matir bhūtvā śṛṇu dharmān mayoditān ||21||**

**dānaṁ dadyād yajed devān yajñaiḥ svādhyāya-tatparaḥ |**  
**nityodakī bhaved vipraḥ kuryāc cāgni-parigraham ||22||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tatra brāhmaṇasyāvaśyakān dharmānāha—dānam iti | dadyāt kuryāt, nityodakī nityaṁ snānatarpaṇādikṛt, yathādhikāramaupāsanāgnestretādīnāṁ vā parigrahaḥ ||22||

**vṛtty-arthaṁ yājayec cānyānanyān adhyāpayet tathā |**  
**kuryāt pratigrahādānaṁ śuklārthān nyāyato dvijaḥ ||23||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: dhanopārjananiyamānāha—vṛttyartham iti | pratigrahādānaṁ pratigrāhyasya gavāderādānaṁ grahaṇaṁ, gurvarthaṁ gurorartho yasmin tat śuklārthāditi pāṭhe tu śuklaḥ śuddhaḥ artho yasya tasmād viprādeḥ | 

kramāgataṁ prītidāyaṁ prāptañca saha bhāryayā |   
aviśeṣeṇa sarveṣāṁ dhanaṁ śuklamudāhṛtam | iti viṣṇuvacanāt | 

śuklārtham iti pāṭhe śukladhanopārjananimittamityarthaḥ | tatrāpi nyāyataḥ kālapuruṣādipratigrahaṁ vinā, dvijo brāhmaṇaḥ ||23||

**sarva-bhūta-hitaṁ kuryān nāhitaṁ kasyacid dvijaḥ |**  
**maitrī samasta-bhūteṣu brahmaasyottamaṁ dhanam ||24||**

**grāvṇi ratne ca pārakye sama-buddhir bhaved dvijaḥ |**  
**ṛtāv abhigamaḥ patnyāṁ śasyate cāsya pārthiva ||25||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: grāve iti | grāve pāṣāṇe pārakye pārakīye ratne vā asya brāhmaṇasyetyupalakṣaṇam | patnyām ṛtau cābhigamaḥ śasyate śrutyābhyanujñāyate, na tu niyamyate | ṛtau bhāryāmupeyāt iti śrutau parisaṁkhyāyā uktatvāt parisaṁkhyāniyamayorbhedāt | tārhi bhaṭṭapādaḥ 

vidhiratyantamaprāptau niyamaḥ pākṣike sati |   
tatra cānyatra ca prāptau parisaṁkhyeti gīyate || 

ityasyārthaḥ svargopāyabhūtajyotiṣṭomasyātyantamaprāptasya prāpaṇaṁ vidhiḥ, pathāgniṣṭomena yajetetyādiḥ | pākṣikaprāptau satyāmaprāptāṁśasya paripūraṇāya niyamena prāpaṇaṁ niyamavidhiḥ, yathā brīhīnavahantītyatra vituṣīkaraṇasyāvahananena nakhanikṛntanādinā ca prāptasya nakhanikṛntanādipakṣe'pi avahananasyāprāptasyāṁśasya niyamena prāpaṇaṁ vidheyasya, tatra cānyatra ca prāptiyogyatāyāṁ anyataranivṛttaye punaḥ prāpaṇaṁ parisaṁkhyā | yathā pañca pañca nakhābhakṣyāḥ \- ṛtau bhāryāmupeyāt iti | atra pañcanakhabhakṣaṇāderlokata eva prāptasya ajñātatvābhāvāt tatra smṛterajñātajñāpakatvalakṣaṇasya prāmāṇyasya asambhavena svārthatyāgāt pañcāririktapañcanakhabhakṣaṇaniṣedhādirūpānyārthakalpanaṁ yuktam, tatra uktarūpaprāmāṇyasattvāt tadanurodhena rāgataḥ prāptasya bādho'pi nyāyya eva | ata eva na svārthatyāgānyārthakalpananiṣedhapratiyogiprāpaka pramāṇabādhalakṣaṇadoṣatrayavattvam | evaṁ śrautodāharaṇe'pi imāmagṛbhnanraśanāmṛtasyetyaśvābhidhānīmādatta ityatra ṛtaphalasādhāraṇāśvamedhasambandhinaḥ paśo raśanāṁ gṛhītavanta ityevamarthakasya mantrasyārthaprakāśanasāmarthyalakṣaṇaliṅgenāśvaraśanā'dāne gardabhādiraśanādāne cobhayatra śrutyanumānadvārā prāpsyataḥ prāgevāśvaraśanā'dāne mantraviniyogalakṣaṇasya śrutyarthasya aprāptasya sattvena śruteraprāptaprāpakatvalakṣaṇaprāmāṇyasambhavānna  
tadanurodhena svārthatyāgastataścānyārthakalpanāprāptabādhaśca nāstīti na doṣatrayagandho'pi | tarhi ajñātajñāpakatvalakṣaṇaprāmāṇyasya sarvatrāviśeṣādapūrvaniyamaparisaṁkhyāvidhīnāṁ ko bheda iti cenna, pramāṇāntarāyogye upāye apūrvavidhiḥ, pākṣikaprāpte niyamavidhiḥ, śrutyapekṣayā vilambitapratyāyakapramāṇenobhayaprāptiyogyatayā parisaṁkhyāvidhiriti pūrvamevoktatvāt | athāpūrvavidhivat parisaṁkhyāvidherapi aprāptaprāpakatvena caritārthatvādanyanivṛttiḥ phalaṁ na syāditi cenna, liṅgena prāpsyato'rthasya śrutyā pūrvapratipādanavaiyarthyādanyanivṛttiphalasyāvaśyakatvāt | tathāpi śrutyā aśvaraśanā'dāne viniyuktasya mantrasya paścālliṅgena viniyogāsambhavādanyanivṛttiḥ, sutarāṁ siddhaiva raśanaiva parisaṁkhyāphalam | apūrvavidhestu agniṣṭomādiṣu pravṛttijananasya sambhavānnānyaphalākāṅketi | ata eva bhaṭṭapādāḥ svayamāhustatra vārtike—

ajñātavidhirevāyamato mantrasya niścitaḥ |   
parisaṁkhyāphalenoktā na viśeṣaḥ punaḥ śruteḥ || 

iti parisaṁkhyānyavṛttiḥ phalamityarthaḥ | tat kuta ityatrāha—na viśeṣa punaḥ śruteḥ iti, liṅgajanyabhaviṣyat punaḥśravaṇasya tat prathamabhavaśrutijanyaśravaṇasya pravṛttilakṣaṇaphalamātre viśeṣābhāvāt śrutijanyaśravaṇasyānyanivṛttirūpa-phalamastyevetyeva kalpanīyamityarthaḥ | kecittu bhaṭṭamate parisaṁkhyāyāḥ smārttodāharaṇaṁ nāstīti vadanti, tanna, pañca pañcanakhā bhakṣyāḥ ityādiṣu uktaprakāreṇa doṣatrayābhāvāt parisaṁkhyodāharaṇatve'pi adoṣād bhedenaiva parisaṁkhyālakṣaṇasya sāmānyenoktatvācca | evam ṛtau bhāryāmupeyāt ityatra ṛtukālānṛtukālayornityavat prāptatayā aprāptāṁśapūraṇalakṣaṇaphalābhāvānniyamavidhyasambhavena parisaṁkhyaiva | tarhi—

ṛtusnātāntu yo bhāryāṁ sannidhau nopagacchati |   
ghorāyāṁ bhrūṇahatyāyāṁ pacyate nātra saṁśayaḥ | 

iti doṣaśravaṇaṁ na syāt | naiṣa doṣaḥ, manasi kāme satyapi tasya dveṣādinā tāmanupagacchato doṣaśravaṇopapatteriti saṁkṣepaḥ | loke vyavāyāmiṣamadyasevā, nityāstu jantornahi tatra codanā | ityādiśukokteśca ||25||

**dānāni dadyād icchāto dvijebhyaḥ kṣatriyo’pi vā |**  
**yajec ca vividhair yajñair adhīyīta ca pārthivaḥ ||26||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: kṣatriyadharmānāha—dānāni iti caturbhiḥ ||26|| 

**śastrājīvo mahī-rakṣā pravarā tasya jīvikā |**  
**tatrāpi prathamaḥ kalpaḥ pṛthivī-paripālanam ||27||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: śastrājīvo yuddhajīvikā, tasya prathame kalpe pakṣe pṛthivīpālanaṁ karmābhidhīyata iti śeṣaḥ || 27||

**dhāritrī-pālanenaiva kṛta-kṛtyā narādhipāḥ |**  
**bhavanti nṛpater aṁśā yato yajñādi-karmaṇām ||28||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: atra hetuḥ dharitri iti | bhavanti nṛpateraṁśāḥ \- puṇyāt ṣaḍguṇamādatte nyāyataḥ paripālayan ityādismṛteḥ svayamekenānuṣṭhitadharmāt pratipālitaviprādyanuṣṭhitadharmaṣaṣṭhāṁśo bhūyāditi bhāvaḥ ||28||

**duṣṭānāṁ śāsanād rājā śiṣṭānāṁ paripālanāt |**  
**prāpnoty abhimatān lokān varṇa-saṁsthāṁ karoti yaḥ ||29||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: varṇānāṁ saṁsthā maryādā tāṁ karotīti tathā | varṇasaṁskāraka iti pāṭhe saṁskārako guṇādhānakartā ||29||

**pāśupālyaṁ ca vāṇijyaṁ kṛṣiṁ ca manujeśvara |**  
**vaiśyāya jīvikāṁ brahmā dadau loka-pitāmahaḥ ||30||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vaiśyadharmānapyāha—pāśupālyam iti dvābhyām ||30||

**tasyāpy adhyayanaṁ yajño dānaṁ dharmaś ca śasyate |**  
**nitya-naimittikādīnāṁ anuṣṭhānaṁ ca karmaṇām ||31||**

**dvijāti-saṁśritaṁ karma tādarthyaṁ tena poṣaṇam |**  
**traya-vikrayajair vāpi dhanaiḥ kārūdbhavena vā ||32||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: śūdrāṇāmapyāha—dvijāti iti | dvijātisaṁśrayaṁ traivarṇikaśuśrūṣālakṣaṇaṁ karma, tādarthaṁ tatpāratantryañca svadharmaḥ | tena dvijaśuśrūṣālabdhenātmapoṣaṇaṁ mukhyam | āpadi tu krayavikrayajairvāṇijyalabdhaiḥ tadasambhave takṣādikārukarmodbhavena dravyeṇa poṣaṇaṁ śūdrasya | dvijaśuśrūṣayā jīvanna hīyate iti śukokteḥ ||32||

**śūdrasya sannatiḥ śaucaṁ sevā svāminy amāyayā |**  
**amantra-yajño hy asteyaṁ sat-saṅgo vipra-rakṣaṇam ||33||**

**dānaṁ ca dadyāc chūdro’pi pāka-yajñair yajeta ca |**  
**pitry-ādikaṁ ca tat sarvaṁ śūdraḥ kurvīta tena vai ||34||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: pākayajñairvaiśvadevākhyaiḥ | namaskāreṇa mantreṇa pañca yajñānna hāpayet iti yājñavalkyokteḥ pitryādikaṁ śrāddhādi | tena dvijaśuśrūṣālabdhena dravyeṇa kurvīta ||34||

**bhṛtyādi-bharaṇārthāya sarveṣāṁ ca parigrahaḥ |**  
**ṛtu-kāle’bhigamanaṁ sva-dāreṣu mahī-pate ||35||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: punaḥ sarveṣāṁ sādhāraṇadharmānāha—bhṛtyādi iti akṣaradvayādhikaiḥ sārdhaistribhiḥ ete | parigrahādyāḥ sarveṣāṁ sāmānyalakṣaṇā iti caturthenānvayaḥ | parigraho'rthasampādanam ||35||

**dayā samasta-bhūteṣu titikṣā nātimānitā |**  
**satyaṁ śaucam anāyāso maṅgalaṁ priya-vāditā ||36||**

**maitrya-spṛhā tathā tadvad akārpaṇyaṁ nareśvara |**  
**anasūyā ca sāmānya-varṇānāṁ kathitā guṇāḥ ||37||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: dayā paraduḥkhapraharaṇecchā, titikṣā śītoṣṇādidvandvasahiṣṇutā, anabhimānitā ātmani śreṣṭhatvādyabhimānaśūnyatā, satyaṁ yathārthakathanam, śaucam mṛjjalābhyāṁ smṛtaṁ bāhyaṁ bhāvaśuddhistathāntaram tat dvividham | 

śarīraṁ pīḍyate yena suśubhenāpi karmaṇā |   
atyantaṁ tanna kurvīta anāyāsaḥ sa ucyate || 

ityanāyāsaḥ | maṅgalam śiraḥ sapuṣpaṁ caraṇau supūjitau ityuktam | maitrī sarvamitrabhāvena varttanam, aspṛhā prāṇayātrāmātranimittādanyatrānabhilāṣaḥ | 

atyuṣṇāt saghṛtādannādacchidrāccaiva vāsasaḥ |   
aparapreṣyabhāvācca nūya icchan patatyadhaḥ || iti | 

akārpaṇyaṁ yathāśakti dānam anasūyā guṇeṣu doṣāropābhāvaḥ ||37||

**āśramāṇāṁ ca sarveṣāṁ ete sāmānya-lakṣaṇāḥ |**  
**guṇāṁs tathāpad-dharmāṁś ca viprādīnāṁ imān śṛṇu ||38||**

**kṣātraṁ karma dvijasyoktaṁ vaiśyaṁ karma tathāpadi |**  
**rājanyasya ca vaiśyoktaṁ śūdra-karma na caitayoḥ ||39||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: uktarītyā vaiśyaśūdrakarmaprāptau taniṣedhamāha etayoḥ kṣatriyavaiśyayoḥ, brāhmaṇasyāpyupalakṣaṇam ||39||

**sāmarthye sati tat tyājyam ubhābhyām api pārthiva |**  
**tad evāpadi kartavyaṁ na kuryāt karma-saṅkaram ||40||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: ubhābhyāṁ kṣatriyavaiśyābhyāṁ, brāhmaṇenāpi atra śaktasya mukhyakalpanirbandhaḥ, aśaktasyānukalpāśrayaḥ eva | karmasaṅkaraṁ vṛttyovyatikaram ||40|| 

**ity ete kathitā rājan varṇa-dharmā mayā tava |**  
**dharmān āśramiṇāṁ samyag bruvato me niśāmaya ||41||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: uktānuvādapūrvakam āśramadharmān vaktuṁ pratijānīte iti iti ||41|| 

iti śrīdhara-svāmi-kṛtāyām ātma-prakāśākhyāyāṁ svaprakāśākhyāyāṁ vā śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇa-ṭīkāyāṁ tṛtīyāṁ'śe aṣṭamo'dhyāyaḥ ||

iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe tṛtīyāṁśe aṣṭamo’dhyāyaḥ

—o)0(o—

(3.9)



## **brahmacaryādy-āśrama-catuṣṭaya-varṇanam**

**aurva uvāca—**  
**bālaḥ kṛtopanayano vedāharaṇa-tatparaḥ |**  
**guru-gehe vased bhūpa brahmacārī samāhitaḥ ||1||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: nirucya haritoṣārthān varṇadharmānaśeṣataḥ | tattadāśramadharmāśca navame'tra nirūpitāḥ ||1||

**śaucācāra-vrataṁ tatra kāryaṁ śuśrūṣaṇaṁ guroḥ |**  
**vratāni caratā grāhyo vedaś ca kṛta-buddhinā ||2||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vratāni prājāpatyaṁ tathā saumyamāgneyaṁ vaiśvadaivikam ityādīni madhumāṁsavarjanādīni ca caratā kurvatā vedo grāhyaḥ ||2||

**ubhe sandhye raviṁ bhūpa tathaivāgniṁ samāhitaḥ |**  
**upatiṣṭhet tadā kuryād guror apy abhivādanam ||3||**

**sthite tiṣṭhed vrajed yāte nīcair āsīta cāsati |**  
**saṁhito guror nṛpa-śreṣṭha pratikūlaṁ na sañcaret ||4||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: sthite ūrdhībhūte gurau śiṣyastiṣṭhet ūrdhībhavet, tathā āsati āsīne nīcaiḥ hīnabhāvenāsīta, pratikūlametadviparītaṁ na kuryāt ||4||

**tenaivoktaṁ paṭhed vedaṁ nānya-cittaḥ puraḥ-sthitaḥ |**  
**anujñātaś ca bhikṣānnam aśnīyād guruṇā tataḥ ||5||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tenaivoktaḥ paṭhet na tu śīghrādhyāpanāya guruṁ niyuñjīta ||5|| 

**avagāhed apaḥ pūrvam ācāryeṇāvagāhitāḥ |**  
**samij-jalādikaṁ cāsya kalyaṁ kalyam upānayet ||6||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: ācāryeṇāvagāhitā apo'vagāhe | kalyaṁ kalyaṁ prātaḥ prātaḥ ||6||

**gṛhīta-grāhya-vedaś ca tato’nujñām avāpya ca |**  
**gārhasthyam āviśet prājño niṣpanna-guru-niṣkṛtiḥ ||7||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: gṛhīto grāhyo grahaṇārho vedo yena saḥ | niṣpannaguruniṣkṛtiḥ dattagurudakṣiṇaḥ ||7||

**vidhināvāpta-dāras tu dhanaṁ prāpya sva-karmaṇā |**  
**gṛhastha-kāryam akhilaṁ kuryād bhūpāla śaktitaḥ ||8||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vidhinā brāhmārṣādinā, svakarmaṇā yājanādinā ||8|| 

**nivāpena pitṝn arcan yajñair devāṁs tathātithīn |**  
**annair munīṁś casvādhyāyair apatyena prajāpatim ||9||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: nivāpena piṇḍadānādinā, pitṛniti pitṛyajño darśitaḥ, yajñairdevāniti devayajñaḥ, atithīnannairiti manuṣyayajñaḥ, munīṁśca svādhyāyairiti brahmayajñaḥ, apatyena prajāpatim iti prasaṅgād gṛhasthasyāvaśyakaṁ karttavyamityuktam ||9||

**bhūtāni balibhiś caiva vairāgylakṣaṇenākhilaṁ jagat |**  
**prāpnoti lokān puruṣo nija-karma-samarjitān ||10||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: balikarmaṇā bhūtānīti bhūtayajñaḥ | vāksatyena satyavacanena | vātsalyeneti pāṭhe dātṛtvenopakartṛtvena vā ||10||

**bhikṣā-bhujaś ca ye kecit parivrāḍ brahmacāriṇaḥ |**  
**te’py atraiva pratiṣṭhante gārhasthyaṁ tena vai param ||11||**

**vedāharaṇa-kāryāya tīrtha-snānāya ca prabho |**  
**aṭanti vasudhāṁ viprāḥ pṛthivī-darśanāya ca ||12||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: aṭanti bhrāmyanti ||12||

**aniketā hy anāhārā yatra sāyaṁ-gṛhāś ca ye |**  
**teṣāṁ gṛhasthaḥ sarveṣāṁ pratiṣṭhā yonir eva ca ||13||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: aniketāḥ agṛhāḥ, ānāhārāḥ ahārārthaṁ sañcayarahitāḥ, yatra sāyaṁ tatraiva gṛhaṁ yeṣāṁ te, pratiṣṭhā āśrayaḥ, yonirmātā sasnehamannadānādinā dehapoṣakatvāt ||13||

**teṣāṁ svāgata-dānādi vaktavyaṁ madhuraṁ nṛpa |**  
**gṛhāgatānāṁ dadyāc ca śayanāsana-bhojanam ||14||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: atasteṣāṁ gṛhāgatānāṁ svāgatoktipūrvakaṁ madhuraṁ priyaṁ vaktavyam ||14||

**atithir yaḥ sa bhagnāśo gṛhāt pratinvartate |**  
**sa dattvā duṣkṛtaṁ tasmai puṇyam ādāya gacchati ||15||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: sa bhagnāśo'tithistasmai pāpaṁ dattveti nityakarmarūpātithipūjābhāvena pratyavāyotpatteḥ | puṇyamādāyeti tatpūjājanyapuṇyānutpatterevamupacaryate ||15||

**avajñānam ahaṅkāro dambhaś caiva gṛhe sataḥ |**  
**paritāpopaghātau ca pāruṣyaṁ ca na śasyate ||16||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: ahaṅkāra ātmanyutkarṣabuddhiḥ | dambho lābhādyaryaṁ dharmācaraṇam | paritāpo vṛthā dattamityurutāpaḥ | upaghātaḥ pratighātaḥ tāḍanaṁ vā | pāruṣyaṁ niṣṭhuratā ||16|| 

**yas tu samyak karoty evaṁ gṛhasthaḥ paramaṁ vidhim |**  
**sarva-bandha-vinirmukto lokān ānoty anuttamān ||17||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: sarvabandhairvimuktaḥ san ||17|| 

**vayaḥ-pariṇato rājan kṛtakṛtyo gṛhāśramī |**  
**putreṣu bhāryāṁ nikṣipya vanaṁ gacchet sahaiva vā ||18||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: kṛtaṁ kṛtyaṁ gṛhocitaṁ yena saḥ ||18|| 

**parṇa-mūla-phalāhāraḥ keśa-śmaśru-jaṭādharaḥ |**  
**bhūmi-śāyī bhavet tatra muniḥ sarvātithir nṛpa ||19||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: sarvātithiḥ sarvātithipūjakaḥ | atithirajñātapūrvaḥ ||19|| 

**carma-kāśa-kuśaiḥ kuryāt paridhānottarīyake |**  
**tadvat triṣavaṇaṁ snānaṁ śastamasya nareśvara ||20||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: trisavanaṁ trikālasnānam, abhyāgato'jñātapūrvaḥ ||20|| 

**devatābhyarcanaṁ homaḥ sarvabhyāgata-pūjanam |**  
**bhikṣā bali-pradānaṁ ca śastamasya nareśvara ||21||**

**vanya-snehena gātrāṇāṁ abhyaṅgaś cāsya śasyate |**  
**tapaś ca tasya rājendra śītoṣṇādi-sahiṣṇutā ||22||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vanyasnehena iṅgu dītailādinā | tapasyatastapaścarataḥ ||22|| 

**yas tv enāṁ niyataś caryāṁ vānaprasthaś caren muniḥ |**  
**sa dahaty agnivad doṣān jayel lokāṁś ca śāśvatān ||23||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: japet prāpnuyāt ||23|| 

**caturthaś cāśramo bhikṣoḥ procyate yo manīṣibhiḥ |**  
**tasya svarūpaṁ gadato mama śrotuṁ nṛpārhasi ||24||**

**putra-dravya-kalatreṣu tyakta-sneho narādhipa |**  
**caturtham āśrama-sthānaṁ gacchen nirdhūta-matsaraḥ ||25||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: caturthamāśramaṁ sthānaṁ viśrāmahetuḥ ||25||
